### [42] [From Haystack to Needle: Label Space Reduction for Zero-shot Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2502.08436)
*Nathan Vandemoortele,Bram Steenwinckel,Femke Ongenae,Sofie Van Hoecke*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为标签空间缩减（LSR）的新方法，用于提高大型语言模型（LLM）的零样本分类性能。LSR通过系统地对候选类别进行排序和缩减来迭代地优化分类标签空间，从而使模型能够专注于最相关的选项。该方法利用无标签数据和数据驱动模型的统计学习能力，在测试时动态优化标签空间表示。在七个基准测试上的实验表明，与标准的零样本分类基线相比，LSR在Llama-3.1-70B上平均提高了7.0%（最高14.2%），在Claude-3.5-Sonnet上平均提高了3.3%（最高11.1%）。为了降低LSR的计算开销，提出了一种将模型蒸馏为概率分类器的方法，从而实现高效推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的零样本分类方法在处理大规模标签空间时面临挑战，容易导致性能下降。研究的动机是开发一种能够有效管理和优化标签空间的方法，以提升大型语言模型（LLM）在零样本分类任务上的表现，尤其是在标签数量庞大时。

Method: LSR方法通过迭代地对候选标签进行排序和缩减来优化标签空间。首先，利用LLM对数据点和标签进行初步评分，然后根据评分对标签进行排序，并移除低分标签，从而缩小标签空间。在迭代过程中，通过利用无标签数据和数据驱动模型的统计学习能力，动态地优化标签空间表示。为了解决LSR的计算成本问题，研究人员提出将LLM蒸馏成一个概率分类器，以实现更高效的推理。

Result: 在七个基准测试上的实验结果显示，LSR在Llama-3.1-70B模型上平均将宏F1分数提高了7.0%（最高提升14.2%），在Claude-3.5-Sonnet模型上平均提高了3.3%（最高提升11.1%）。与标准的零样本分类基线相比，LSR显著提升了分类性能。

Conclusion: LSR是一种有效提高LLM零样本分类性能的新方法，尤其在处理大规模标签空间时表现出色。通过迭代优化标签空间和引入蒸馏技术，LSR在提升准确性的同时，也考虑了计算效率。未来的工作可以探索LSR在更多领域和模型上的应用，并进一步优化其计算效率。

Abstract: We present Label Space Reduction (LSR), a novel method for improving
zero-shot classification performance of Large Language Models (LLMs). LSR
iteratively refines the classification label space by systematically ranking
and reducing candidate classes, enabling the model to concentrate on the most
relevant options. By leveraging unlabeled data with the statistical learning
capabilities of data-driven models, LSR dynamically optimizes the label space
representation at test time. Our experiments across seven benchmarks
demonstrate that LSR improves macro-F1 scores by an average of 7.0% (up to
14.2%) with Llama-3.1-70B and 3.3% (up to 11.1%) with Claude-3.5-Sonnet
compared to standard zero-shot classification baselines. To reduce the
computational overhead of LSR, which requires an additional LLM call at each
iteration, we propose distilling the model into a probabilistic classifier,
allowing for efficient inference.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Verdict库采用模块化推理单元（如验证、辩论和聚合）的组合方式，并增加推理时计算量，以提高LLM裁判的质量。该方法通过组合不同的推理策略来增强评估能力，并利用更多的计算资源来获得更精确的结果。

Result: 在内容审核、事实核查和幻觉检测等具有挑战性的任务上，Verdict裁判的表现与更大规模的微调裁判、提示裁判和推理模型相比具有竞争力。这表明Verdict在提高LLM裁判性能方面是有效的。

Conclusion: Verdict库为研究人员和实践者提供了一个可扩展、可解释且可靠的基于LLM的评估系统的基础。该框架通过模块化设计和计算增强，有效解决了LLM裁判的可靠性问题，并在多项评估任务中取得了优异的成绩。

Abstract: The use of LLMs as automated judges ("LLM-as-a-judge") is now widespread, yet
standard judges suffer from a multitude of reliability issues. To address these
challenges, we introduce Verdict, an open-source library for scaling judge-time
compute to enhance the accuracy, reliability, and interpretability of automated
evaluators. Verdict leverages the composition of modular reasoning units (such
as verification, debate, and aggregation) and increased inference-time compute
to improve LLM judge quality. Across a variety of challenging tasks such as
content moderation, fact-checking, and hallucination detection, Verdict judges
achieves performance competitive with orders-of-magnitude larger fine-tuned
judges, prompted judges, and reasoning models. Our framework establishes a
foundation for scalable, interpretable, and reliable LLM-based evaluation
systems for both researchers and practitioners.

### [44] [Assessing the Macro and Micro Effects of Random Seeds on Fine-Tuning Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2503.07329)
*Nghia Bui,Guergana Savova,Lijing Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 随机种子对大型语言模型（LLMs）的微调影响被忽视，本研究系统评估了随机种子在GLUE和SuperGLUE基准测试中的影响。通过宏观指标（准确率、F1值）的均值和方差以及微观指标（预测一致性）的分析，发现随机种子在宏观和微观层面都存在显著的变异性，强调了在微调和评估LLMs时考虑随机种子的重要性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究系统地评估了随机种子对LLMs微调的影响。在GLUE和SuperGLUE基准测试中，通过计算传统指标（准确率、F1值）的均值和方差来评估宏观层面的影响，并引入了新的指标“一致性”来衡量模型在不同随机种子下的预测稳定性，以捕捉微观层面的影响。

Conclusion: 随机种子对LLMs的微调和评估过程至关重要。本研究揭示了随机种子在宏观和微观层面的显著影响，强调了在进行LLMs的研究和应用时，必须仔细考虑和报告随机种子的选择。未来的工作可以进一步探索缓解随机种子影响的策略，并研究其在更广泛的模型和任务上的效应。

Abstract: The impact of random seeds in fine-tuning large language models (LLMs) has
been largely overlooked despite its potential influence on model performance.In
this study, we systematically evaluate the effects of random seeds on LLMs
using the GLUE and SuperGLUE benchmarks. We analyze the macro-level impact
through traditional metrics like accuracy and F1, calculating their mean and
variance to quantify performance fluctuations. To capture the micro-level
effects, we introduce a novel metric, consistency, measuring the stability of
individual predictions across runs. Our experiments reveal significant variance
at both macro and micro levels, underscoring the need for careful consideration
of random seeds in fine-tuning and evaluation.

### [45] [Traversal Verification for Speculative Tree Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.12398)
*Yepeng Weng,Qiao Hu,Xujie Chen,Li Liu,Dianwen Mei,Huishi Qiu,Jiang Tian,Zhongchao Shi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Speculative decoding uses a draft model to predict multiple future tokens, which are then verified in parallel by the target model. Existing methods struggle with suboptimal acceptance length and inefficient verification due to their top-down, token-level approach. This paper introduces Traversal Verification, a new algorithm that verifies sequences from leaf-to-root, preserving valid subsequences and guaranteeing lossless inference. Experiments show it improves acceptance length and throughput over existing methods.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Large language models (LLMs) are computationally expensive, and speculative decoding offers a way to speed them up by using a smaller draft model to predict future tokens, which are then verified by the main model. However, current speculative decoding frameworks face challenges: 1) Their token-level verification doesn't fully align with sequence-level probabilities, leading to shorter accepted sequences than potentially possible. 2) The top-down verification process is inefficient; if a parent node is rejected, all its descendants are discarded, wasting computation. This research addresses these limitations to make speculative decoding more effective.

Method: The paper proposes Traversal Verification, a novel algorithm for speculative decoding. Unlike existing top-down methods, Traversal Verification employs a leaf-to-root traversal strategy. It considers the entire sequence from a potential end point back to the current node. This allows it to identify and preserve valid subsequences even if parts of the sequence higher up the tree are rejected. The theoretical analysis demonstrates that this approach yields the same probability distribution as the original target model, ensuring accuracy. Experiments were conducted using various LLMs and multiple tasks to evaluate the performance against existing methods.

Result: Experimental results demonstrate that Traversal Verification significantly outperforms existing speculative decoding methods. The key findings indicate consistent improvements in acceptance length, meaning more speculative tokens are accepted on average. Furthermore, the method achieves higher throughput, signifying faster generation speeds. These gains were observed across different LLM architectures and diverse downstream tasks, highlighting the robustness and generalizability of the proposed approach.

Conclusion: Traversal Verification represents a significant advancement in speculative decoding for LLMs. By introducing a leaf-to-root verification paradigm, it overcomes the limitations of previous methods, achieving lossless inference with substantial acceleration. The improved acceptance length and throughput shown in experiments validate its effectiveness. This work paves the way for more efficient deployment and utilization of large language models.

Abstract: Speculative decoding is a promising approach for accelerating large language
models. The primary idea is to use a lightweight draft model to speculate the
output of the target model for multiple subsequent timesteps, and then verify
them in parallel to determine whether the drafted tokens should be accepted or
rejected. To enhance acceptance rates, existing frameworks typically construct
token trees containing multiple candidates in each timestep. However, their
reliance on token-level verification mechanisms introduces two critical
limitations: First, the probability distribution of a sequence differs from
that of individual tokens, leading to suboptimal acceptance length. Second,
current verification schemes begin from the root node and proceed layer by
layer in a top-down manner. Once a parent node is rejected, all its child nodes
should be discarded, resulting in inefficient utilization of speculative
candidates. This paper introduces Traversal Verification, a novel speculative
decoding algorithm that fundamentally rethinks the verification paradigm
through leaf-to-root traversal. Our approach considers the acceptance of the
entire token sequence from the current node to the root, and preserves
potentially valid subsequences that would be prematurely discarded by existing
methods. We theoretically prove that the probability distribution obtained
through Traversal Verification is identical to that of the target model,
guaranteeing lossless inference while achieving substantial acceleration gains.
Experimental results across different large language models and multiple tasks
show that our method consistently improves acceptance length and throughput
over existing methods.

</details>


### [46] [Does Synthetic Data Help Named Entity Recognition for Low-Resource Languages?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.16814)
*Gaurav Kamath,Sowmya Vajjala*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了在标签数据有限的低资源语言中，使用合成数据进行命名实体识别（NER）的有效性。研究结果表明，合成数据对低资源语言NER有积极作用，但其效果因语言而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低资源语言的命名实体识别（NER）由于缺乏标注数据，一直是一个挑战。数据增强，特别是利用合成数据，是解决这一问题的常用方法，因此研究合成数据在低资源NER中的作用具有重要意义。

Method: 该研究针对11种来自不同语系的低资源语言，探索了合成数据在多语言NER任务中的应用。通过实验评估合成数据对NER系统性能的影响。

Result: 研究发现在低资源语言NER任务中，合成数据确实显示出提升性能的潜力。然而，不同语言之间合成数据带来的效果存在显著差异，表明其适用性并非普遍一致。

Abstract: Named Entity Recognition(NER) for low-resource languages aims to produce

of multilingual, low-resource NER, considering 11 languages from diverse
language families. Our results suggest that synthetic data does in fact hold
promise for low-resource language NER, though we see significant variation
between languages.

### [47] [The Case for Repeatable, Open, and Expert-Grounded Hallucination Benchmarks in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.17345)
*Justin D. Norman,Michael U. Rivera,D. Alex Hughes*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 模型生成的文本中存在不准确的“幻觉”现象被认为普遍存在且对负责任地采用语言模型构成问题。然而，目前缺乏科学研究来全面衡量这种现象的普遍性。本文主张应采用可重复、开放且与领域相关的幻觉基准测试来评估语言模型。研究提出了一个幻觉分类法，并通过案例研究表明，在数据创建的早期阶段缺乏专家参与会导致幻觉指标缺乏有效性和实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型在生成文本时可能出现不准确、捏造的信息（即“幻觉”）的现象，这种现象被广泛认为普遍存在，并对负责任地部署和使用语言模型构成了重大障碍。尽管存在这种担忧，但目前科学界对于如何全面、系统地衡量语言模型幻觉的普遍性和严重程度的研究还很有限。这种衡量上的不足，使得我们难以准确评估风险，也阻碍了有效的缓解策略的开发。因此，有必要建立一种科学、可重复的方法来评估语言模型的幻觉问题。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于可重复、开放且领域上下文的幻觉基准测试方法来评估语言模型。研究人员开发了一个幻觉的分类体系，以结构化地识别和理解不同类型的幻觉。此外，他们进行了一个案例研究，强调了在数据创建过程中，缺乏领域专家的早期参与会对幻觉指标的有效性和实用性产生负面影响。该案例研究旨在说明在数据标注和评估过程中，专业知识的重要性。

Result: 案例研究表明，当专家未能在数据创建的早期阶段介入时，所产生的幻觉指标在有效性和实际应用方面存在显著缺陷。具体来说，缺乏专业知识的评估可能导致对幻觉的识别不准确或不全面，从而使得评估结果失去可靠性，无法为改进模型提供有价值的指导。这突显了在构建和使用幻觉基准测试时，专业知识不可或缺。

Conclusion: 本文强调了使用可重复、开放且与领域相关的基准测试来评估语言模型幻觉的重要性。通过案例研究，论文证明了在数据创建早期阶段缺乏专家参与会严重损害幻觉指标的有效性和实用性。因此，未来的研究和实践应重视专家在整个评估流程中的作用，以确保开发出更可靠、更有用的评估工具，从而推动语言模型朝着更负责任的方向发展。研究的局限性在于案例研究的范围可能有限，未来的工作可以扩展到更多领域和模型，并探索更自动化的专家知识整合方法。

Abstract: Plausible, but inaccurate, tokens in model-generated text are widely believed
to be pervasive and problematic for the responsible adoption of language
models. Despite this concern, there is little scientific work that attempts to
measure the prevalence of language model hallucination in a comprehensive way.
In this paper, we argue that language models should be evaluated using
repeatable, open, and domain-contextualized hallucination benchmarking. We
present a taxonomy of hallucinations alongside a case study that demonstrates
that when experts are absent from the early stages of data creation, the
resulting hallucination metrics lack validity and practical utility.

### [48] [Distilling LLM Agent into Small Models with Retrieval and Code Tools](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.17612)
*Minki Kang,Jongwon Jeong,Seanie Lee,Jaewoong Cho,Sung Ju Hwang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“Agent Distillation”的框架，旨在将大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力和完整的任务解决行为（包括使用检索和代码工具）转移到小型语言模型（sLMs）中。通过引入“first-thought prefix”提示方法和“self-consistent action generation”技术，显著提升了蒸馏的质量和sLMs在推理任务中的鲁棒性。实验结果表明，即使是0.5B参数的小型模型，也能在多种推理任务上达到与更大模型相媲美的性能，证明了Agent Distillation在构建实用的、能够使用工具的小型智能体方面的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂的推理任务中表现出色，但其高昂的计算成本限制了实际应用。现有的将LLMs的推理能力蒸馏到小型语言模型（sLMs）中的方法（如使用Chain-of-Thought（CoT）轨迹）在处理需要罕见事实知识或精确计算的任务时效果不佳，sLMs容易出现“幻觉”现象。因此，需要一种更有效的方法来将LLMs的完整任务解决能力，特别是利用检索和代码工具的能力，转移到计算资源受限的sLMs中。

Method: 该研究提出了Agent Distillation框架，包含两个主要改进：1. **First-thought prefix**：一种新的提示方法，用于增强教师LLM生成的推理轨迹（trajectories）的质量，使其包含更多有用的中间步骤和思考过程。2. **Self-consistent action generation**：一种在测试时提高小型智能体（sLMs）鲁棒性的方法，可能通过生成多个动作候选项并选择最一致的动作来实现。该方法在八个跨事实和数学领域的推理任务上进行了评估，涵盖了域内和域外泛化能力。

Result: 在八个推理任务上的实验结果表明，经过Agent Distillation蒸馏的小型语言模型（sLMs），即使参数量仅为0.5B、1.5B和3B，也能在性能上与使用CoT蒸馏的下一级别（1.5B、3B、7B参数）的模型相媲美。这证明了Agent Distillation在将LLM的工具使用能力和推理能力有效迁移到小型模型上的能力。

Conclusion: Agent Distillation框架能够有效地将大型语言模型（LLMs）的完整任务解决行为（包括工具使用）迁移到小型语言模型（sLMs）中，显著提升了小型模型在复杂推理任务上的性能和鲁棒性。即使是参数量很小的模型，也能在Agent Distillation的帮助下，在各种推理任务上达到与更大模型相当的水平，这为开发实用、经济高效的工具使用型小型智能体开辟了新的途径。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在更多类型任务和工具上的应用，以及优化蒸馏过程以适应更广泛的模型和应用场景。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) excel at complex reasoning tasks but remain
computationally expensive, limiting their practical deployment. To address
this, recent works have focused on distilling reasoning capabilities into
smaller language models (sLMs) using chain-of-thought (CoT) traces from teacher
LLMs. However, this approach struggles in scenarios requiring rare factual
knowledge or precise computation, where sLMs often hallucinate due to limited
capability. In this work, we propose Agent Distillation, a framework for
transferring not only reasoning capability but full task-solving behavior from
LLM-based agents into sLMs with retrieval and code tools. We improve agent
distillation along two complementary axes: (1) we introduce a prompting method
called first-thought prefix to enhance the quality of teacher-generated
trajectories; and (2) we propose a self-consistent action generation for
improving test-time robustness of small agents. We evaluate our method on eight
reasoning tasks across factual and mathematical domains, covering both
in-domain and out-of-domain generalization. Our results show that sLMs as small
as 0.5B, 1.5B, 3B parameters can achieve performance competitive with next-tier
larger 1.5B, 3B, 7B models fine-tuned using CoT distillation, demonstrating the
potential of agent distillation for building practical, tool-using small
agents. Our code is available at https://github.com/Nardien/agent-distillation.

### [49] [R2R: Efficiently Navigating Divergent Reasoning Paths with Small-Large Model Token Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.21600)
*Tianyu Fu,Yi Ge,Yichen You,Enshu Liu,Zhihang Yuan,Guohao Dai,Shengen Yan,Huazhong Yang,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLMs推理开销大，SLMs效率高但推理路径不同。R2R仅在关键路径发散时才使用LLM，大部分由SLM处理。通过自动生成数据训练路由，R2R结合R1-1.5B和R1-32B，在数学、编程和QA基准上，以5.6B平均激活参数优于7B模型1.6倍，并与32B模型相当但速度快2.8倍，提升了效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）虽然推理能力强大，但存在显著的推理开销，给部署带来挑战。蒸馏得到的小型语言模型（SLMs）效率更高，但由于未能遵循LLMs的推理路径，其性能有所下降。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Roads to Rome (R2R)”的神经令牌路由方法。该方法通过识别LLMs和SLMs之间推理路径产生分歧的关键令牌，仅对这些令牌启用LLM进行处理，而将大部分令牌生成任务交给SLM。为了训练一个轻量级的路由器，研究者开发了一个自动数据生成流程，用于识别分歧令牌并生成令牌级别的路由标签。

Result: 将R2R应用于DeepSeek家族的R1-1.5B和R1-32B模型，并在数学、编程和问答基准上进行了评估。结果显示，在平均激活参数量为5.6B的情况下，R2R的准确率平均比R1-7B高1.6倍，甚至优于R1-14B模型。与R1-32B模型相比，R2R实现了2.8倍的实际运行时间加速，同时保持了相当的性能，有效提升了测试时扩展效率的帕累托前沿。

Conclusion: R2R方法通过选择性地利用LLM处理关键的路径发散令牌，显著提高了效率，同时保持了高质量的输出。该方法在多个基准测试中表现出色，证明了其在解决LLM部署挑战方面的潜力。未来的工作可以探索更复杂的路由策略和应用于更大规模的模型。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) achieve impressive reasoning capabilities at the
cost of substantial inference overhead, posing substantial deployment
challenges. Although distilled Small Language Models (SLMs) significantly
enhance efficiency, their performance suffers as they fail to follow LLMs'
reasoning paths. Luckily, we reveal that only a small fraction of tokens
genuinely diverge reasoning paths between LLMs and SLMs. Most generated tokens
are either identical or exhibit neutral differences, such as minor variations
in abbreviations or expressions. Leveraging this insight, we introduce **Roads
to Rome (R2R)**, a neural token routing method that selectively utilizes LLMs
only for these critical, path-divergent tokens, while leaving the majority of
token generation to the SLM. We also develop an automatic data generation
pipeline that identifies divergent tokens and generates token-level routing
labels to train the lightweight router. We apply R2R to combine R1-1.5B and
R1-32B models from the DeepSeek family, and evaluate on challenging math,
coding, and QA benchmarks. With an average activated parameter size of 5.6B,
R2R surpasses the average accuracy of R1-7B by 1.6x, outperforming even the
R1-14B model. Compared to R1-32B, it delivers a 2.8x wall-clock speedup with
comparable performance, advancing the Pareto frontier of test-time scaling
efficiency. Our code is available at https://github.com/thu-nics/R2R.

</details>


### [50] [Read Your Own Mind: Reasoning Helps Surface Self-Confidence Signals in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.23845)
*Jakub Podolak,Rajeev Verma*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究分析了 DeepSeek R1-32B 模型在问答任务中的不确定性来源，发现模型自我报告的口头置信度常过于乐观，而通过采样多重回答得到的语义熵则更可靠。研究表明，增加测试时计算量，例如通过强制模型进行长链式思考，能显著提升其口头置信度的有效性。此外，另一个独立的阅读器模型仅通过链式思考即可重建类似的置信度，这表明口头置信度可能只是推理过程中产生的替代方案的统计数据。最终结论是，可靠的不确定性估计需要显式探索生成空间，并且只有在进行此类探索后，自我报告的置信度才值得信赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不确定性估计是评估大型语言模型（LLM）可靠性的关键环节。然而，LLM 在问答任务中常常表现出自相矛盾的行为：一方面，它们能够生成流畅且看似自信的回答；另一方面，它们在面对不确定性时，其自我报告的置信度往往不可靠，甚至出现过度自信的现象。理解并解决 LLM 不确定性估计的来源和可靠性问题，对于确保模型在关键应用中的安全和有效性至关重要。本研究旨在深入分析 DeepSeek R1-32B 模型在问答任务中不确定性估计的不足之处，特别是其口头置信度的局限性，并探索提高其不确定性估计可靠性的方法。

Method: 本研究采用问答任务作为实验平台，分析 DeepSeek R1-32B 模型的不确定性来源。研究对比了两种不确定性估计方法：1. **默认的“先回答后置信度”设置**：模型直接给出答案，并附带自我报告的口头置信度。2. **语义熵**：通过采样模型的大量回答来计算，这需要更多的测试时计算量来探索模型的预测分布。为了验证计算量对置信度的影响，研究采用了“强制长链式思考”的策略，即要求模型在给出最终答案前，先生成一个详细的推理过程。此外，研究还训练了一个独立的阅读器模型，仅输入链式思考过程，观察其是否能重建与原模型相似的置信度。

Result: 研究发现，在默认的“先回答后置信度”设置下，DeepSeek R1-32B 模型经常表现出过度自信。相比之下，通过采样多重回答计算得到的语义熵，即使在简单的、通常不需要推理的事实检索问题上，也能提供更可靠的不确定性估计。强制模型进行长链式思考的实验表明，当模型有更多计算预算来探索其预测分布时，其口头置信度的有效性得到了显著提升。另外，独立的阅读器模型仅通过分析推理过程（链式思考）就能重构出非常相似的置信度分数，这暗示了口头置信度可能仅仅是推理过程中涌现出的各种可能性的一种统计衡量。

Conclusion: 本研究得出结论，可靠的不确定性估计需要模型能够显式地探索其生成空间，而不仅仅依赖于表面的自我报告。DeepSeek R1-32B 模型在问答任务中，其自我报告的口头置信度只有在经过充分的生成空间探索（例如通过长链式思考）后才变得值得信赖。这项发现强调了在评估和应用大型语言模型时，需要对模型的不确定性估计机制进行更深入的分析，并可能需要设计新的方法来促使模型进行更充分的探索，从而获得更准确、更可靠的不确定性度量。本研究的局限性可能在于实验仅限于特定的模型和任务，未来的工作可以扩展到更多模型和更广泛的应用场景，并进一步探索有效的探索机制。

Abstract: We study the source of uncertainty in DeepSeek R1-32B by analyzing its
self-reported verbal confidence on question answering (QA) tasks. In the
default answer-then-confidence setting, the model is regularly over-confident,
whereas semantic entropy - obtained by sampling many responses - remains
reliable. We hypothesize that this is because of semantic entropy's larger
test-time compute, which lets us explore the model's predictive distribution.
We show that granting DeepSeek the budget to explore its distribution by
forcing a long chain-of-thought before the final answer greatly improves its
verbal score effectiveness, even on simple fact-retrieval questions that
normally require no reasoning. Furthermore, a separate reader model that sees
only the chain can reconstruct very similar confidences, indicating the verbal
score might be merely a statistic of the alternatives surfaced during
reasoning. Our analysis concludes that reliable uncertainty estimation requires
explicit exploration of the generative space, and self-reported confidence is
trustworthy only after such exploration.

</details>


### [51] [LexTime: A Benchmark for Temporal Ordering of Legal Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04041)
*Claire Barale,Leslie Barrett,Vikram Sunil Bajaj,Michael Rovatsos*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了LexTime数据集，用于评估大型语言模型（LLMs）在法律文本中事件排序的能力。研究发现LLMs在处理法律事件排序方面优于普通叙事文本，但法律文本的复杂性仍然是一个挑战。研究为改进LLMs在法律领域的时序事件推理能力提供了方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基准测试在处理法律文本的事件时间关系方面存在不足，缺乏专门的语言评估，这阻碍了对LLMs在法律领域事件排序能力理解。理解和准确重建事件时间线对于案例法分析、合规性监控和法律摘要至关重要。

Method: 研究创建了一个名为LexTime的数据集，包含512个来自美国联邦诉状的实例，并标注了事件对及其时间关系。使用该数据集来评估LLMs在法律文本中的事件排序能力。

Result: 研究结果表明：1. LLMs在处理法律事件排序方面的准确率比普通叙事文本高出10.5%。2. 较长的输入上下文和隐含事件能够提高准确率，其中隐含-显式事件对的准确率达到80.8%。3. 法律语言的复杂性和嵌套从句仍然是LLMs面临的挑战。

Conclusion: 尽管LLMs在法律事件排序方面表现出潜力，但法律文本的特定复杂性仍然是法律时序事件推理的瓶颈。研究提出了具体的建模方向，以期更好地解决这些挑战，并为未来在法律领域改进LLMs的时序推理能力奠定了基础。

Abstract: Understanding temporal relationships and accurately reconstructing the event
timeline is important for case law analysis, compliance monitoring, and legal
summarization. However, existing benchmarks lack specialized language
evaluation, leaving a gap in understanding how LLMs handle event ordering in
legal contexts. We introduce LexTime, a dataset designed to evaluate LLMs'
event ordering capabilities in legal language, consisting of 512 instances from
U.S. Federal Complaints with annotated event pairs and their temporal
relations. Our findings show that (1) LLMs are more accurate on legal event
ordering than on narrative texts (up to +10.5%); (2) longer input contexts and
implicit events boost accuracy, reaching 80.8% for implicit-explicit event
pairs; (3) legal linguistic complexities and nested clauses remain a challenge.
While performance is promising, specific features of legal texts remain a
bottleneck for legal temporal event reasoning, and we propose concrete modeling
directions to better address them.

</details>


### [52] [Scalable Medication Extraction and Discontinuation Identification from Electronic Health Records Using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.11137)
*Chong Shao,Douglas Snyder,Chiran Li,Bowen Gu,Kerry Ngan,Chun-Ting Yang,Jiageng Wu,Richard Wyss,Kueiyu Joshua Lin,Jie Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究评估了大型语言模型（LLMs）在电子健康记录（EHR）中提取药物信息和识别停药情况的能力，特别关注了在无人工标注情况下的可扩展性。研究发现，GPT-4o在零样本设置下表现最佳，在药物提取、停药分类和联合任务中均取得了最高的F1分数。开源模型紧随其后，Llama-3.1-70B-Instruct在特定数据集上表现优异。医疗领域专用LLMs的表现不如通用LLMs。少量样本学习通常能提升性能，而思维链（CoT）推理的效果不一。总体而言，LLMs在EHR药物信息提取和停药识别方面展现出巨大潜力，开源模型提供了可扩展的替代方案，且少量样本学习能进一步增强其能力。

Result: 研究发现，LLMs在从EHR笔记中提取药物和分类停药情况方面表现出有希望的性能。在零样本设置下，GPT-4o在所有任务中始终获得最高的平均F1分数：药物提取为94.0%，停药分类为78.1%，联合任务为72.7%。开源模型紧随其后，Llama-3.1-70B-Instruct在MIV-Med数据集的药物状态分类（68.7%）以及在Re-CASI（76.2%）和MIV-Med（60.2%）数据集的联合任务中取得了最高性能。医疗领域专用LLMs的表现低于先进的通用领域LLMs。少量样本学习通常能提升性能，而思维链（CoT）推理带来的性能提升效果不一。

Abstract: Identifying medication discontinuations in electronic health records (EHRs)

open-sourced and proprietary large language models (LLMs) in extracting

potential for medication extraction and discontinuation identification on EHR

### [53] [Post Persona Alignment for Multi-Session Dialogue Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.11857)
*Yi-Pei Chen,Noriki Nishida,Hideki Nakayama,Yuji Matsumoto*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 现有方法在多轮对话中维护长期一致性和个性化响应方面存在挑战。本文提出了一种名为“后 persona 对齐”（PPA）的新型两阶段框架，该框架首先生成一个通用的对话响应，然后利用该响应查询并检索相关 persona 信息，最后对响应进行优化以确保其与说话者的 persona 一致。这种“后对齐”策略在保持一致性和个性化的同时，提高了响应的自然度和多样性。实验证明，PPA 在一致性、多样性和 persona 相关性方面显著优于现有方法，为长期个性化对话生成提供了一个更灵活有效的范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮个性化对话生成面临长期一致性和生成多样化、个性化响应的挑战。大型语言模型（LLMs）虽然在单轮对话中表现出色，但在保持跨多轮交互中的 persona 准确性和对话连贯性方面存在困难。现有的方法通常在生成响应前检索 persona 信息，这可能限制响应的多样性并导致输出通用化。

Method: 本文提出的“后 persona 对齐”（PPA）是一个新颖的两阶段框架。第一阶段：仅基于对话上下文生成一个通用的响应。第二阶段：利用上一步生成的响应作为查询，检索相关的 persona 记忆。最后，对生成的响应进行优化，使其与说话者的 persona 对齐。

Result: 在多轮 LLM 生成的对话数据集上进行的实验表明，PPA 在一致性、多样性和 persona 相关性方面显著优于现有方法。PPA 提供了一种更灵活、更有效的长期个性化对话生成范式。

Conclusion: PPA 通过其创新的“后对齐”策略，有效解决了多轮个性化对话生成中的长期一致性和多样性挑战。该方法在实验中取得了优于现有方法的性能，证明了其在提升对话自然度、个性化和连贯性方面的潜力。PPA 为未来的个性化对话系统提供了一个有前途的框架。

Abstract: Multi-session persona-based dialogue generation presents challenges in
maintaining long-term consistency and generating diverse, personalized
responses. While large language models (LLMs) excel in single-session
dialogues, they struggle to preserve persona fidelity and conversational
coherence across extended interactions. Existing methods typically retrieve
persona information before response generation, which can constrain diversity
and result in generic outputs. We propose Post Persona Alignment (PPA), a novel
two-stage framework that reverses this process. PPA first generates a general
response based solely on dialogue context, then retrieves relevant persona
memories using the response as a query, and finally refines the response to
align with the speaker's persona. This post-hoc alignment strategy promotes
naturalness and diversity while preserving consistency and personalization.
Experiments on multi-session LLM-generated dialogue data demonstrate that PPA
significantly outperforms prior approaches in consistency, diversity, and
persona relevance, offering a more flexible and effective paradigm for
long-term personalized dialogue generation.

### [54] [AlphaDecay: Module-wise Weight Decay for Heavy-Tailed Balancing in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14562)
*Di He,Songjun Tu,Ajay Jaiswal,Li Shen,Ganzhao Yuan,Shiwei Liu,Lu Yin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Weight decay, a common regularization method for LLMs, usually uses a uniform decay rate for all layers. This paper introduces AlphaDecay, which adaptively assigns different weight decay strengths to each module based on Heavy-Tailed Self-Regularization (HT-SR) theory. Modules with heavy-tailed spectral densities (indicating stronger feature learning) get weaker decay, while those with lighter tails get stronger decay. This approach improves perplexity and generalization across various model sizes (60M to 1B) compared to uniform decay and other adaptive methods.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard weight decay in LLM training uses a uniform decay rate for all layers, ignoring the diverse structures and spectral properties of different modules. This can lead to suboptimal regularization. The paper aims to address this by proposing an adaptive weight decay strategy that accounts for these module-specific characteristics, potentially improving model performance and generalization.

Method: The proposed method, AlphaDecay, is guided by Heavy-Tailed Self-Regularization (HT-SR) theory. It analyzes the empirical spectral density (ESD) of weight correlation matrices within each module to quantify its 'heavy-tailedness'. Modules with more pronounced heavy-tailed ESDs, suggesting stronger feature learning, are assigned weaker weight decay. Conversely, modules with lighter-tailed spectra are assigned stronger decay. This tailored approach aims to balance module-wise spectral property differences.

Result: Extensive pre-training experiments were conducted on models ranging from 60 million to 1 billion parameters. The results demonstrate that AlphaDecay consistently achieves better perplexity and generalization performance compared to conventional uniform weight decay and other existing adaptive decay baselines. This indicates the effectiveness of the adaptive decay strategy.

Conclusion: AlphaDecay offers a simple yet effective method for improving LLM training by adaptively assigning weight decay strengths based on module-specific spectral properties, guided by HT-SR theory. The method shows significant improvements in perplexity and generalization across various model sizes. Future work could explore its application in fine-tuning or other model architectures, and further investigate the theoretical underpinnings of HT-SR in deep learning.

Abstract: Weight decay is a standard regularization technique for training large
language models (LLMs). While it is common to assign a uniform decay rate to
every layer, this approach overlooks the structural diversity of LLMs and the
varying spectral properties across modules. In this paper, we introduce
AlphaDecay, a simple yet effective method that adaptively assigns different
weight decay strengths to each module of an LLM. Our approach is guided by
Heavy-Tailed Self-Regularization (HT-SR) theory, which analyzes the empirical
spectral density (ESD) of weight correlation matrices to quantify
"heavy-tailedness." Modules exhibiting more pronounced heavy-tailed ESDs,
reflecting stronger feature learning, are assigned weaker decay, while modules
with lighter-tailed spectra receive stronger decay. Our method leverages
tailored weight decay assignments to balance the module-wise differences in
spectral properties, leading to improved performance. Extensive pre-training
tasks with various model sizes from 60M to 1B demonstrate that AlphaDecay
achieves better perplexity and generalization than conventional uniform decay
and other adaptive decay baselines. Our code is available at
https://github.com/hed-ucas/AlphaDecay.

</details>


### [55] [Omni-Router: Sharing Routing Decisions in Sparse Mixture-of-Experts for Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.05724)
*Zijin Gu,Tatiana Likhomanenko,Navdeep Jaitly*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为Omni-router Transformer的新型混合专家（MoE）模型，用于自动语音识别（ASR）。与传统MoE模型中各层独立路由不同，Omni-router Transformer通过共享跨层路由器来增强专家间的协作和专业化，从而在降低训练损失的同时，显著优于密集模型和Switch Transformer模型，平均词错误率分别降低了11.2%和8.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的混合专家（MoE）模型在语言建模领域取得了成功，但将其应用于自动语音识别（ASR）时，存在专家选择缺乏跨层协作的问题。现有MoE方法（如Switch Transformer）在各层独立路由，导致路由器在不同层面的选择相关性不强，未能充分发挥专家间的协同作用，限制了模型的性能提升和专业化程度。

Method: 本研究提出了一种名为Omni-router Transformer的新模型。该模型的核心创新在于引入了一个共享的路由器，该路由器跨越不同的MoE层。这种设计旨在增强不同层级专家之间的协作，并促进更深层次的专业化。通过共享路由器，模型能够更有效地整合来自不同层级的专家信息，从而实现更优的语音识别性能。实验在大型伪标签数据集上进行，并在10个不同的、非领域内的ASR基准测试集上进行了评估。

Result: Omni-router Transformer在大型伪标签数据集上实现了较低的训练损失。在10个多样化的、非领域内的ASR基准测试中，Omni-router Transformer持续优于传统的密集模型和Switch Transformer模型。具体而言，与密集模型相比，平均词错误率（WER）降低了11.2%；与Switch Transformer相比，平均WER降低了8.2%。此外，该模型还展现了结构化的专家使用方式和对多样化数据的改进鲁棒性。

Conclusion: Omni-router Transformer通过引入共享跨层路由器，成功解决了传统MoE模型在ASR任务中专家协作不足的问题。该模型不仅在训练损失和词错误率方面取得了显著的改进，还提供了结构化的专家利用和更强的鲁棒性。这表明共享路由器的设计是提升MoE模型在ASR领域性能的有效途径。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的共享路由机制或与其他模型架构的结合。

Abstract: Mixture-of-experts (MoE) architectures have expanded from language modeling
to automatic speech recognition (ASR). Traditional MoE methods, such as the
Switch Transformer, route experts independently within each layer. Our analysis
reveals that routers in most layers make expert choices that are not strongly
correlated with the choices of the routers in other layers. To increase the
cooperation between experts in different layers and encourage greater
specialization, we use a shared router across different MoE layers. We call
this model Omni-router Transformer. Extensive experiments on a large-scale
pseudo-labeled dataset and evaluations across 10 diverse, out-of-domain ASR
benchmarks demonstrate that the Omni-router Transformer is able to achieve
lower training loss and consistently outperform dense and Switch Transformer
models, reducing average word error rates by 11.2% and 8.2%, respectively,
while providing structured expert usage and improved robustness to diverse
data.

*Xiaoyuan Li,Moxin Li,Wenjie Wang,Rui Men,Yichang Zhang,Fuli Feng,Dayiheng Liu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验结果显示，尽管MLLM在多模态数学推理方面取得了进展，但在执行细粒度视觉操作方面，其表现与人类相比仍存在显著差距。具体来说，模型在代码生成和编辑（特别是修改和注释等精细操作）方面需要进一步改进，才能满足复杂多模态数学推理的需求。

Conclusion: 本研究首次系统性地评估了MLLM在多模态数学推理中基于代码的视觉操作能力，揭示了当前模型在该领域的局限性。研究提出的评估框架和数据集为后续研究提供了基准。未来的工作应致力于提升MLLM在精确代码生成和细粒度视觉编辑方面的能力，以实现更可靠和强大的多模态数学推理。

Abstract: Recent progress in Multi-modal Large Language Models (MLLMs) has enabled
step-by-step multi-modal mathematical reasoning by performing visual operations
based on the textual instructions. A promising approach uses code as an
intermediate representation to precisely express and manipulate the images in
the reasoning steps. However, existing evaluations focus mainly on text-only

addressing that gap by evaluating MLLM's code-based capabilities in multi-modal
mathematical reasoning.Specifically, our framework focuses on two key
evaluation aspects: (1) Multi-modal Code Generation (MCG) evaluates the model's
ability to accurately understand and construct visualizations from scratch. (2)
Multi-modal Code Editing (MCE) assesses the model's capacity for fine-grained
operations, which include three types: Deletion, Modification and Annotation.
To evaluate the above tasks, we incorporate a dataset that covers the five most
popular types of mathematical figures, including geometric diagrams, function
plots, and three types of statistical charts, to provide a comprehensive and
effective measurement of existing MLLMs. Our experimental evaluation involves

significantly behind human performance in performing fine-grained visual
operations.

### [58] [Sparse-dLLM: Accelerating Diffusion LLMs with Dynamic Cache Eviction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.02558)
*Yuerong Song,Xiaoran Liu,Ruixiao Li,Zhigeng Liu,Zengfeng Huang,Qipeng Guo,Ziwei He,Xipeng Qiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 扩散式大语言模型（dLLMs）在推理和并行解码方面取得了突破，但存在推理时高昂的二次计算复杂度和内存开销问题。现有缓存技术通过存储全层状态来加速解码，但内存占用大，限制了长上下文应用。本研究提出的Sparse-dLLM框架通过动态缓存淘汰与稀疏注意力相结合，实现了高达10倍的吞吐量提升，同时保持了相当的性能和峰值内存消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散式大语言模型（dLLMs）在处理长文本时面临计算复杂度和内存开销的挑战，现有缓存技术虽然能加速解码，但内存占用过高，限制了其在长上下文场景下的应用。因此，需要一种更有效的缓存策略来解决这些问题。

Method: Sparse-dLLM框架通过分析dLLMs的注意力模式，发现跨层存在稀疏性，关键token在解码过程中保持显著性，低相关性token则保持不重要。基于此，提出了一种训练无关的框架，结合了动态缓存淘汰和稀疏注意力机制，通过延迟双向稀疏缓存，保留关键token并动态淘汰不重要的前缀/后缀条目。

Result: 在LLaDA和Dream系列上的广泛实验表明，Sparse-dLLM实现了高达10倍于原始dLLMs的吞吐量，同时保持了相当的性能和相似的峰值内存成本，在效率和效果上均优于先前的方法。

Conclusion: Sparse-dLLM作为首个集成动态缓存淘汰与稀疏注意力的训练无关框架，有效解决了dLLMs在长上下文处理中的效率问题，实现了显著的吞吐量提升，同时保持了性能和内存占用的平衡。

Abstract: Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) enable breakthroughs in reasoning and
parallel decoding but suffer from prohibitive quadratic computational
complexity and memory overhead during inference. Current caching techniques
accelerate decoding by storing full-layer states, yet impose substantial memory
usage that limit long-context applications. Our analysis of attention patterns
in dLLMs reveals persistent cross-layer sparsity, with pivotal tokens remaining
salient across decoding steps and low-relevance tokens staying unimportant,
motivating selective cache eviction. We propose Sparse-dLLM, the first
training-free framework integrating dynamic cache eviction with sparse
attention via delayed bidirectional sparse caching. By leveraging the stability
of token saliency over steps, it retains critical tokens and dynamically evicts
unimportant prefix/suffix entries using an attention-guided strategy. Extensive
experiments on LLaDA and Dream series demonstrate Sparse-dLLM achieves up to
10$\times$ higher throughput than vanilla dLLMs, with comparable performance
and similar peak memory costs, outperforming previous methods in efficiency and
effectiveness. The code is available at
https://github.com/OpenMOSS/Sparse-dLLM.

</details>


### [59] [A Survey on Collaborating Small and Large Language Models for Performance, Cost-effectiveness, Cloud-edge Privacy, and Trustworthiness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.13890)
*Fali Wang,Jihai Chen,Shuhua Yang,Ali Al-Lawati,Linli Tang,Hui Liu,Suhang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种对小语言模型（SLM）和大语言模型（LLM）协作的系统性调查，该调查从协作目标的角度出发，旨在解决LLM在微调成本、推理延迟、边缘部署和可靠性方面的挑战。研究提出了一个涵盖性能增强、成本效益、云边隐私和可信赖性四个目标的分类体系，并回顾了代表性方法、总结了设计范式，最后概述了实现高效和安全SLM-LLM协作的开放性挑战和未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）在各个领域取得了显著进展，但它们也面临着微调成本高、推理延迟大、边缘部署受限以及可靠性不足等挑战。小型语言模型（SLM）因其体积小、效率高和适应性强的特点，为解决这些问题提供了有前景的方案。本研究的动机在于，通过整合SLM的专业化和效率与LLM的泛化和推理能力，构建协作框架，以应对不同任务和部署场景下的多样化目标，从而克服LLM的局限性。

Method: 本研究提出了一种从协作目标角度对SLM-LLM协作进行系统性调查的方法。研究首先构建了一个包含四个主要目标的分类体系：性能增强、成本效益、云边隐私和可信赖性。随后，在该框架下，对该领域的代表性方法进行了回顾和梳理，总结了实现SLM-LLM协作的设计范式，并分析了当前存在的挑战以及未来可能的研究方向。

Result: 本文对SLM-LLM协作的研究进行了系统性的梳理，重点关注了四个关键的协作目标：性能增强、成本效益、云边隐私和可信赖性。研究回顾了实现这些目标的相关方法和技术，总结了不同的设计范式，并为如何高效、安全地实现SLM与LLM的协同工作提供了见解。然而，具体的量化结果、性能指标对比以及详细的实验设置并未在摘要中详细说明，这部分内容需要在论文正文中进一步探究。

Conclusion: 本研究系统性地 survey 了SLM-LLM协作领域，并提出了一个有价值的分类体系，为理解和推动该领域的研究提供了框架。通过解决LLM面临的成本、效率、部署和可靠性等挑战，SLM-LLM协作展现出巨大的潜力。尽管摘要中未详述具体的技术细节和实验结果，但该 survey 指出了未来的研究方向，强调了在高效和安全方面实现SLM-LLM协作的重要性，并为该领域的进一步发展奠定了基础。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable progress across domains
and applications but face challenges such as high fine-tuning costs, inference
latency, limited edge deployability, and reliability concerns. Small language
models (SLMs), with compact, efficient, and adaptable features, offer promising
solutions. Building on this potential, recent research explores collaborative
frameworks that integrate their complementary strengths, leveraging SLMs'
specialization and efficiency with LLMs' generalization and reasoning to
address diverse objectives across tasks and deployment scenarios. Motivated by
these developments, this paper presents a systematic survey of SLM-LLM
collaboration from the perspective of collaboration objectives. We propose a
taxonomy covering four goals: performance enhancement, cost-effectiveness,
cloud-edge privacy, and trustworthiness. Under this framework, we review
representative methods, summarize design paradigms, and outline open challenges
and future directions toward efficient and secure SLM-LLM collaboration. The
collected papers are available at https://github.com/FairyFali/SLMs-Survey.

</details>

### [60] [Wide frequency-range acceleration using second harmonic RF bucket in fixed field accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03226)
*Tomonori Uesugi,Yoshihiro Ishi,Yoshiharu Mori*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的固定场加速器（FFA）加速方案，结合了谐波数为 h=1 和 h=2 的射频（RF）桶，通过时序组合形成单一连续的加速路径，从而在两次射频频率扫描中完成加速，减小了总频率扫描范围并缩短了重复周期。通过 Kyoto 大学辐射核科学研究所 (KURNS) 的 FFA 参数进行纵向模拟，证明了该方法的可行性，并确定了第二谐波 RF 桶保持稳定和可用的运行条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固定场加速器（FFA）在加速粒子时面临挑战，尤其是在需要宽频率范围和较长重复周期的情况下。现有技术难以在保证粒子束稳定的同时实现高效加速。因此，需要一种创新的加速方案来克服这些限制，提高 FFA 的性能和实用性。

Method: 本研究提出了一种新的加速方案，核心在于利用两种不同谐波数（h=1 和 h=2）的射频（RF）空腔。通过精确控制这两种 RF 空腔的时间序列，将它们有效地组合成一条连续的加速路径。这种方法允许在两次射频频率扫描内完成整个加速过程。为了验证方案的可行性，研究人员基于 Kyoto 大学辐射核科学研究所 (KURNS) 的 FFA 参数进行了详细的纵向模拟。模拟的重点是评估粒子束在第二谐波 RF 空腔中的稳定性和可用性，并确定了能够维持这种稳定性的具体运行条件。

Result: 通过基于 KURNS FFA 参数的纵向模拟，研究证实了所提出的结合 h=1 和 h=2 谐波 RF 空腔的时序组合加速方案是可行的。模拟结果表明，该方法能够有效缩短总频率扫描范围并减短加速器的重复周期。此外，研究还确定了确保第二谐波 RF 空腔稳定运行的操作条件，这对于实际应用至关重要。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的新型 FFA 加速方案，通过时序组合 h=1 和 h=2 的射频空腔，成功地缩短了频率扫描范围和重复周期，并验证了其在 KURNS FFA 参数下的可行性。该方案为提高 FFA 的加速效率和性能提供了新的途径，尤其是在第二谐波 RF 空腔的稳定运行方面取得了重要进展。未来的工作可以进一步优化操作条件，并考虑在实际加速器中进行实验验证。

Abstract: We propose a novel acceleration scheme for fixed-field accelerators (FFAs),
in which RF buckets with harmonic numbers $h = 1$ and $h = 2$ are
time-sequenced to form a single, continuous acceleration path. This approach
completes acceleration in two RF frequency sweeps, thereby reducing the total
frequency sweep range and shortening the repetition period. The feasibility of
this method is demonstrated through longitudinal simulations based on
parameters of the FFA at the Institute for Integrated Radiation and Nuclear
Science, Kyoto University (KURNS). We also establish operational conditions
under which the second harmonic RF bucket remains stable and practically
usable.

### [61] [Beam Cleaning and Collimation Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03511)
*Stefano Redaelli*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 大型强子对撞机（LHC）的束流准直系统在控制高能粒子束损失方面达到了前所未有的性能水平，其复杂性和清洁度是其他加速器无法比拟的，对于加速器的可靠运行至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高强度、高能的对撞机（如LHC）运行中会产生不可避免的束流损失，这些损失的能量可能远超超导磁体淬灭所需的能量阈值，甚至能损坏加速器组件。因此，精确控制和安全处理这些束流损失对于确保加速器可靠运行至关重要。

Method: 本文以CERN的LHC为例，详细介绍了其多级束流准直系统的设计。该系统通过多层准直器精确地阻挡和引导偏离束流，以防止其对加速器组件造成损害。

Result: LHC的准直系统实现了前所未有的束流清洁度，能够高效地处理束流损失，确保加速器的安全运行。该系统的复杂性在同类加速器中是最高的。

Conclusion: LHC的准直系统是应对高能、高强度粒子束损耗挑战的典范，展示了复杂准直系统在大型加速器中的设计和运行方面取得的重大进展。未来的研究可进一步探讨其在大规模准直系统设计和运行方面的经验教训。

Abstract: Collimation systems in particle accelerators are designed to safely and
efficiently dispose of unavoidable beam losses during operation. Their specific
roles vary depending on the type of accelerator. The state of the art in hadron
beam collimation for high-intensity, high-energy superconducting colliders is
exemplified by the system implemented at the CERN Large Hadron Collider (LHC).
In this machine, the stored beam energy reaches levels several orders of
magnitude higher than the tiny energy required to quench superconducting
magnets. It also exceeds by orders of magnitude the damage thresholds of
typical accelerator components, placing stringent demands on beam loss control.
Collimation systems are therefore essential for the reliable daily operation of
modern accelerators. This lecture reviews the design of a multistage
collimation system, using the LHC as a case study. The LHC collimation system
has achieved unprecedented cleaning performance, with a level of complexity
unmatched by any other accelerator. Design aspects and operational challenges
of such large-scale collimation systems are also discussed.

### [62] [ALAS: Transactional and Dynamic Multi-Agent LLM Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03094)
*Longling Geng,Edward Y. Chang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 该研究提出了ALAS框架，用于解决大型语言模型（LLM）在多智能体规划中存在的脆弱性问题。ALAS通过将规划与非循环验证分离、记录版本化执行日志以及进行局部修复，显著提高了规划的鲁棒性、效率和可扩展性。实验证明，ALAS在作业车间调度任务上能够达到或超过现有基线，同时大幅减少了计算资源消耗并提高了运行速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大型语言模型（LLM）的多智能体规划方法虽然灵活，但在实际应用中存在诸多问题，包括：验证过程容易出现循环依赖，状态变化难以追踪和修复，以及微小的错误可能导致代价高昂的全局重新计算。这些问题严重限制了LLM在复杂规划任务中的可靠性和效率。

Method: ALAS框架的核心在于其状态化和干扰感知能力。它将规划过程与验证过程分离开来，验证器独立于规划LLM运行，并使用独立、受限的上下文，避免了自检循环和上下文损耗。ALAS还记录了版本化的执行日志，用于进行精确的检查和恢复。当出现故障时，ALAS能够进行局部修复，仅修改最小受影响的区域，并遵循一系列明确定义的策略（如重试、捕获、超时、回退、幂等键、补偿、循环保护等）。这些策略被编码在一种规范的工作流中间表示（IR）中，可以映射到Amazon States Language和Argo Workflows。实验在DMU和TA的作业车间调度套件上，针对五个经典基准进行了测试。

Result: 在作业车间调度任务的五个经典基准测试中，ALAS在成功率上达到或超过了强大的单LLM和多智能体基线，成功率高达83.7%。与同等设置下的基线相比，ALAS的代币使用量减少了60%，运行速度提高了1.82倍。初步的可靠性研究表明，ALAS的验证器能够以较低的开销检测注入的结构性故障，并且局部修复能够在运行时将干扰限制在可接受的范围内，其编辑半径较小，并且与全局重新计算相比，对任务完工时间（makespan）的影响更小。

Conclusion: ALAS框架通过结合独立的验证器、版本化的执行日志和局部修复机制，有效解决了LLM多智能体规划中的脆弱性问题，显著提升了系统的效率、可行性和可扩展性。实验结果表明，ALAS在保持高成功率的同时，大幅降低了计算资源消耗和运行时间。该方法为开发更可靠、更高效的LLM驱动的规划系统提供了有力的支持。未来工作将涉及进一步的性能优化和在更广泛的应用场景中的部署。

Abstract: Large language models enable flexible multi-agent planning but remain fragile
in practice: verification is often circular, state changes are not tracked for
repair, and small faults trigger costly global recomputation. We present ALAS,
a stateful, disruption-aware framework that separates planning from
non-circular validation, records a versioned execution log for grounded checks
and restore points, and performs localized repair that preserves work in
progress. The validator operates independently of the planning LLM with fresh,
bounded context, avoiding self-check loops and mid-context attrition. The
repair protocol edits only the minimal affected region under explicit policies
(retry, catch, timeout, backoff, idempotency keys, compensation, loop guards)
defined in a canonical workflow IR that maps to Amazon States Language and Argo
Workflows. On job-shop scheduling suites (DMU, TA) across five classical
benchmarks, ALAS matches or exceeds strong single-LLM and multi-agent
baselines, achieving 83.7% success, reducing token usage by 60%, and running
1.82times faster under comparable settings. A minimal reliability study shows
that the validator detects injected structural faults with low overhead, and
that localized repair contains runtime perturbations with a bounded edit radius
and less makespan degradation than global recompute. Results indicate that the
combination of validator isolation, versioned execution logs, and localized
repair provides measurable efficiency, feasibility, and scalability for
multi-agent LLM planning. Code and seeds will be released.

</details>


### [63] [Large Language Models Miss the Multi-Agent Mark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.21298)
*Emanuele La Malfa,Gabriele La Malfa,Samuele Marro,Jie M. Zhang,Elizabeth Black,Michael Luck,Philip Torr,Michael Wooldridge*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: MAS LLM 领域存在理论与实践脱节的问题，许多研究忽视了 MAS 的核心原则，如自主性、社会互动和结构化环境。本文旨在通过系统分析，指出现有 MAS LLM 实现的不足，并提出应更好地整合成熟的 MAS 概念和精确的术语，以避免误解和错失研究机会。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 MAS LLM 领域的研究存在一个显著问题：许多框架虽然声称利用了多智能体系统（MAS）的理念，但在实践中却未能真正遵循 MAS 的基本原理。这种现象导致了理论与实践之间的脱节，可能阻碍该领域的健康发展。如果不解决这些根本性问题，未来的研究可能会重复解决 MAS 领域早已处理过的难题，从而浪费资源并减缓进展。因此，深入分析 MAS LLM 的现状，明确其与传统 MAS 理论的差距，并提出改进方向，具有重要的理论和实践意义。

Method: 本文采用系统性分析的方法，深入探讨了当前 MAS LLM 研究中存在的四个关键问题：1. 智能体（agent）的社会性；2. 环境设计；3. 协调与通信协议；4. 涌现行为的度量。通过对比分析MAS理论与现有MAS LLM的实现，揭示了两者之间的差距。研究聚焦于现有MAS LLM在自主性、社会互动和结构化环境等核心MAS特征上的缺失，以及过度依赖以LLM为中心的简化架构。

Result: 研究发现，当前许多 MAS LLM 的实现并未体现出传统 MAS 理论中的关键特征，例如智能体的自主性、智能体之间的社会互动以及在结构化环境中的运行。这些系统往往采用过于简化的、以 LLM 本身为中心的架构，未能充分利用 MAS 的优势。这种偏差可能导致研究方向的偏离，并限制了MAS LLM在解决复杂问题时的潜力和有效性。

Conclusion: 本文认为，MAS LLM 领域需要对其研究方法和术语使用进行反思。为了避免重复研究、提高研究效率并充分发挥 MAS LLM 的潜力，未来的研究应更加注重将成熟的 MAS 理论概念（如自主性、协调机制、环境交互等）融入到 LLM 的设计和实现中。采用更精确的术语和严谨的 MAS 原理，将有助于该领域朝着更健康、更可持续的方向发展，并解锁新的研究机遇。

Abstract: Recent interest in Multi-Agent Systems of Large Language Models (MAS LLMs)
has led to an increase in frameworks leveraging multiple LLMs to tackle complex
tasks. However, much of this literature appropriates the terminology of MAS
without engaging with its foundational principles. In this position paper, we
highlight critical discrepancies between MAS theory and current MAS LLMs
implementations, focusing on four key areas: the social aspect of agency,
environment design, coordination and communication protocols, and measuring
emergent behaviours. Our position is that many MAS LLMs lack multi-agent
characteristics such as autonomy, social interaction, and structured
environments, and often rely on oversimplified, LLM-centric architectures. The
field may slow down and lose traction by revisiting problems the MAS literature
has already addressed. Therefore, we systematically analyse this issue and
outline associated research opportunities; we advocate for better integrating
established MAS concepts and more precise terminology to avoid
mischaracterisation and missed opportunities.

</details>

### [64] [Relativistic multistage resonant and trailing-field acceleration induced by large-amplitude Alfvén waves in a strong magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03069)
*S. Isayama,S. Matsukiyo,T. Sano,S. H. Chen*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: Summary generation failed


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

Abstract: We propose a particle acceleration mechanism driven by large-amplitude
Alfv\'en waves in a strong magnetic field. The acceleration process proceeds
through multiple stages triggered by counterpropagating wave-particle resonant
acceleration (CWRA) via decay instability. Initially, parent and daughter
Alfv\'en waves resonantly accelerate particles perpendicular to the ambient
magnetic field. The resultant modulational instability generates electrostatic
fields within the wave packet, which are locally amplified by the ponderomotive
force of the Alfv\'en wave packet. These fields subsequently drive further
acceleration within a few relativistic gyroperiods via gyroresonant surfing
acceleration (GRSA). During this, the v*B force facilitates momentum transfer
from the perpendicular to the parallel direction. In the later stage, particles
become trapped by the parent wave and gain additional energy through single
wave resonant acceleration (SWRA). Furthermore, the accumulation of accelerated
particles induces electrostatic trailing fields behind and at the tail of the
wave packet, which drive trailing-field acceleration (TFA) of other electrons.
The combined effects of these mechanisms, CWRA followed by GRSA and SWRA,
result in highly relativistic electron energy. The electron energy accelerated
through the above process is higher than that accelerated through TFA. This
multistage acceleration process provides insights into the generation of high
energy cosmic rays in astrophysical environments.

</details>


### [65] [Particle-in-cell simulations of laser crossbeam energy transfer via magnetized ion-acoustic wave](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03090)
*Yuan Shi,John D. Moody*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用二维PIC模拟研究了磁场对激光驱动高密度等离子体中跨束能量转移（CBET）的影响，特别是通过离子声波（IAW）准模介导的CBET。研究发现在磁场存在下，CBET的能量增益会因激光偏振方式的不同而发生显著变化，这与理论预期一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光驱动的高密度系统中常存在磁场，这些磁场不仅影响等离子体状态，还会通过改变波及其非线性相互作用来直接影响激光-等离子体相互作用（LPI）。理解磁场如何影响LPI中的能量转移过程，特别是跨束能量转移（CBET），对于优化激光聚变等高能量密度物理研究至关重要。本文旨在揭示磁场对以离子声波（IAW）准模为媒介的CBET过程的直接影响。

Method: 研究采用二维粒子- in-cell (PIC) 模拟方法，在CBET为主导且处于线性状态（泵浦耗尽、分布函数演化和次级不稳定性不显著）的参数空间内进行。通过傅里叶滤波分离种子信号，并将种子场投影到两个电磁本征模上，这两个本征模在磁化等离子体中会变得简并。通过比较CBET发生前后的种子能量，提取了两种本征模的CBET能量增益，并分析了初始线性偏振激光在不同磁场强度和激光偏振（平行与正交）下的增益变化。

Result: 模拟结果显示，当磁场强度达到兆特斯拉（MG）级别时，两个本征模表现出不同的能量增益。磁化程度影响了增益与激光失谐的依赖关系。当初始激光偏振平行时，整体增益随磁化增强而降低；而当初始激光偏振正交时，原本不存在的增益变得可能。这些发现与理论预期在定性上是一致的。

Conclusion: 本研究通过PIC模拟证实了磁场对CBET过程的显著影响。研究揭示了磁场如何通过改变等离子体中波的行为来调节激光能量在不同波束间的转移效率，特别是在不同激光偏振条件下。这些发现为理解和控制激光-等离子体相互作用中的磁场效应提供了重要的理论依据，并对高能量密度物理和惯性约束聚变等领域具有潜在的应用价值。未来的工作可以进一步探索更广泛的参数空间，包括非线性区域和更复杂的磁场结构，以及考虑其他影响CBET的因素。

Abstract: Large magnetic fields, either imposed externally or produced spontaneously,
are often present in laser-driven high-energy-density systems. In addition to
changing plasma conditions, magnetic fields also directly modify laser-plasma
interactions (LPI) by changing participating waves and their nonlonear
interactions. In this paper, we use two-dimensional particle-in-cell (PIC)
simulations to investigate how magnetic fields directly affect crossbeam energy
transfer (CBET) from a pump to a seed laser beam, when the transfer is mediated
by the ion-acoustic wave (IAW) quasimode. Our simulations are performed in the
parameter space where CBET is the dominant process, and in a linear regime
where pump depletion, distribution function evolution, and secondary
instabilities are insignificant. We use a Fourier filter to separate out the
seed signal, and project the seed fields to two electromagnetic eigenmodes,
which become nondegenerate in magnetized plasmas. By comparing the seed energy
before CBET occurs and after CBET reaches quasi-steady state, we extract CBET
energy gains of both eigenmodes for lasers that are initially linearly
polarized. Our simulations reveal that starting from a few MG fields, the two
eigenmodes have different gains, and magnetization alters how the gains depend
on laser detuning. The overall gain decreases with magnetization when the laser
polarizations are initially parallel, while a nonzero gain becomes allowed when
the laser polarizations are initially orthogonal. These findings qualitatively
agree with theoretical expectations.

</details>


### [66] [First global gyrokinetic profile predictions of ITER burning plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03336)
*A. Di Siena,C. Bourdelle,A. Bañón Navarro,G. Merlo,T. Görler,E. Fransson,A. Polevoi,S. H. Kim,F. Koechl,A. Loarte,E. Fable,C. Angioni,P. Mantica,F. Jenko*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次使用全局回旋动力学模拟了ITER基线运行场景（15 MA），重点研究了从磁轴到rho_tor = 0.6的径向区域。结果显示，电磁涨落调节了明显的密度峰值，预期的聚变增益Q=12.2，符合ITER目标。模拟识别出微撕裂模式、动力学膨胀模式和低波数下的阿尔芬离子温度梯度模式等电磁模式在核心输运中的关键作用，需要高数值分辨率。与全局模拟相比，局部通量管模拟虽然在定性上相似，但对剖面梯度的敏感性更高。外部环向旋转对湍流输运影响甚微，而平坦的q剖面（接近零磁剪切）会加剧湍流输运。尽管电子温度梯度湍流初期较大，但长期来看会被弱阻尼的零星流淬灭。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ITER作为下一代聚变装置，其基线运行场景的等离子体性能预测至关重要。理解并准确模拟该场景下的湍流输运机制，特别是电磁效应和不同等离子体参数（如安全因子、旋转等）的影响，对于实现ITER的设计目标（如Q=12.2的聚变增益）具有直接意义。现有模拟方法在处理全局效应和特定物理过程（如电磁效应）方面存在局限性，因此需要更先进的模拟手段来精确评估ITER的性能。

Method: 本文采用了全局回旋动力学模拟方法，使用GENE-Tango代码，结合静电和电磁模拟。模拟的径向范围覆盖了从磁轴附近到rho_tor = 0.6的区域。研究了湍流谱，分析了各种湍流模式（如微撕裂模式、动力学膨胀模式、阿尔芬离子温度梯度模式）的作用，并比较了全局模拟与局部通量管模拟的结果。同时，研究了外部环向旋转和安全因子剖面对湍流输运的影响，并考虑了低碰撞度下的零星流动力学。

Result: 全局回旋动力学模拟预测ITER基线场景（15 MA）的聚变增益Q=12.2。模拟显示存在明显的密度峰值，并被电磁涨落所调节。核心输运的关键驱动因素包括微撕裂模式、动力学膨胀模式和低波数下的阿尔芬离子温度梯度模式。与全局模拟相比，局部通量管模拟显示出更高的剖面梯度敏感性（更强的刚度）。外部环向旋转对湍流输运的影响可忽略不计。平坦的q剖面（接近零磁剪切）会加剧动力学膨胀模式，显著增加湍流输运。电子温度梯度湍流虽然初期可能很大，但会被弱阻尼的零星流在长期内淬灭。

Conclusion: 本文首次通过全局回旋动力学模拟，为ITER基线运行场景提供了详细的湍流输运分析，并预测了其聚变增益。研究强调了电磁效应、特定的湍流模式（如微撕裂模式、动力学膨胀模式）以及安全因子剖面对核心输运的关键作用。尽管外部旋转影响不大，但平坦的q剖面可能严重影响约束性能。低碰撞度下的零星流对控制湍流具有重要作用。这些结果对于理解和优化ITER的运行至关重要，但也指出了精确模拟需要高数值分辨率，并且局部模拟可能无法完全捕捉全局效应。未来工作可集中于更广泛的参数空间探索和考虑更多物理效应。

Abstract: In this work, we present the first global gyrokinetic simulations of the ITER
baseline scenario operating at 15 MA using GENE-Tango electrostatic and
electromagnetic simulations. The modeled radial region spans close to the
magnetic axis up to rho_tor = 0.6. Our results show a pronounced density
peaking, moderated by electromagnetic fluctuations. The predicted fusion gain
for this scenario is Q = 12.2, aligning well with ITER's mission objectives. We
further characterize the turbulence spectra and find that electromagnetic
modes, such as microtearing modes, kinetic ballooning modes, and Alfvenic ion
temperature gradient modes at low binormal wave numbers, play a critical role
in the core transport of this ITER scenario, necessitating high numerical
resolution for accurate modeling. Local flux-tube simulations qualitatively
reproduce the key features observed in the global gyrokinetic simulations but
exhibit a much higher sensitivity to profile gradients, reflecting increased
stiffness, likely due to the linearization of the equilibrium profiles and
safety factor. Our study also reveals that the imposed external toroidal
rotation profiles have a negligible impact on turbulent transport, as their
magnitudes are substantially lower than the dominant linear growth rates.
Furthermore, we demonstrate that the safety factor profile is of paramount
importance: scenarios featuring flat q profiles with near-zero magnetic shear
lead to the destabilization of kinetic ballooning modes in the plasma core,
significantly enhancing turbulent transport and potentially degrading
confinement. Finally, although electron temperature gradient turbulence
initially appears large, sometimes exceeding ion-scale transport levels, it is
ultimately quenched over long timescales by secular evolution of zonal flows,
which are weakly damped under the very low collisionality conditions expected
in ITER.

</details>

### [67] [PublicAgent: Multi-Agent Design Principles From an LLM-Based Open Data Analysis Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03023)
*Sina Montazeri,Yunhe Feng,Kewei Sha*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLM）在处理开放数据存储库以支持循证决策方面存在局限性。本文提出了PublicAgent，一个多智能体框架，通过将任务分解为专门的智能体来克服这些限制，从而提高了注意力的集中度，并在每个阶段实现了验证。评估结果产生了五个设计原则，强调了专业化、智能体类别（通用与条件）、故障缓解、跨任务复杂性的架构优势以及模型感知架构设计的必要性。该框架旨在通过自然语言接口使更广泛的用户能够访问公共数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放数据存储库虽然对循证决策至关重要，但对于缺乏数据集发现、模式映射和统计分析专业知识的非专家来说，却难以访问。虽然大型语言模型（LLM）在单个任务中显示出潜力，但它们在端到端分析工作流中存在固有的局限性，例如注意力分散、专业推理模式干扰以及错误未被检测到地传播。

Method: 本文提出了PublicAgent，一个多智能体框架，通过将复杂的数据分析任务分解为专门的智能体来解决LLM在端到端分析工作流中的局限性。这些智能体分别负责意图明确、数据集发现、分析和报告。这种架构设计旨在将注意力集中在各个智能体的上下文中，并在分析过程的每个阶段实现验证，从而防止错误累积。研究人员在五个模型和 50 个查询上评估了该框架，以推导出设计原则。

Result: 评估结果产生了五个设计原则：1.专业化独立于模型强度提供价值，即使是最强的模型，其智能体也达到了 97.5% 的胜率，这表明其益处与模型规模无关。2.智能体可分为通用型（发现、分析）和条件型（报告、意图），通用型智能体表现出一致的有效性（标准差 12.4%），而条件型智能体因模型而异（标准差 20.5%）。3.智能体能够缓解不同的故障模式，移除发现或分析智能体会导致灾难性故障（243-280 个实例），而移除报告或意图智能体则会导致质量下降。4.架构优势在不同任务复杂度下得以持续，胜率稳定（分析 86-92%，发现 84-94%），表明其价值在于工作流管理而非推理增强。5.智能体在不同模型之间的效果差异很大（分析为 42-96%），这需要进行模型感知架构设计。

Conclusion: PublicAgent 多智能体框架通过将复杂分析工作流分解为专门的智能体，有效解决了大型语言模型在访问开放数据时面临的挑战。研究得出的五个设计原则强调了专业化的重要性、通用型和条件型智能体的不同行为、故障缓解机制的有效性、架构优势在任务复杂性方面的持久性以及模型感知设计的必要性。这些原则为构建更有效的多智能体 LLM 系统提供了指导，并最终旨在通过自然语言接口拓宽公共数据的可及性。

Abstract: Open data repositories hold potential for evidence-based decision-making, yet
are inaccessible to non-experts lacking expertise in dataset discovery, schema
mapping, and statistical analysis. Large language models show promise for
individual tasks, but end-to-end analytical workflows expose fundamental
limitations: attention dilutes across growing contexts, specialized reasoning
patterns interfere, and errors propagate undetected. We present PublicAgent, a
multi-agent framework that addresses these limitations through decomposition
into specialized agents for intent clarification, dataset discovery, analysis,
and reporting. This architecture maintains focused attention within agent
contexts and enables validation at each stage. Evaluation across five models
and 50 queries derives five design principles for multi-agent LLM systems.
First, specialization provides value independent of model strength--even the
strongest model shows 97.5% agent win rates, with benefits orthogonal to model
scale. Second, agents divide into universal (discovery, analysis) and
conditional (report, intent) categories. Universal agents show consistent
effectiveness (std dev 12.4%) while conditional agents vary by model (std dev
20.5%). Third, agents mitigate distinct failure modes--removing discovery or
analysis causes catastrophic failures (243-280 instances), while removing
report or intent causes quality degradation. Fourth, architectural benefits
persist across task complexity with stable win rates (86-92% analysis, 84-94%
discovery), indicating workflow management value rather than reasoning
enhancement. Fifth, wide variance in agent effectiveness across models (42-96%
for analysis) requires model-aware architecture design. These principles guide
when and why specialization is necessary for complex analytical workflows while
enabling broader access to public data through natural language interfaces.

</details>


### [68] [No-Human in the Loop: Agentic Evaluation at Scale for Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03051)
*Tao Zhang,Kehui Yao,Luyi Ma,Jiao Chen,Reza Yousefi Maragheh,Kai Zhao,Jianpeng Xu,Evren Korpeoglu,Sushant Kumar,Kannan Achan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了ScalingEval，一个大规模的LLM评测基准研究，系统性地比较了36个LLM在多个产品类别的表现。研究采用了共识驱动的评估协议，通过多智能体框架聚合模式审计和问题代码，生成“事实标签”，实现了在无人工标注的情况下可复现地比较LLM评测能力。主要发现包括：Anthropic Claude 3.5 Sonnet 决策置信度最高；Gemini 1.5 Pro 在跨类别综合表现最佳；GPT-4o 在延迟-准确性-成本权衡方面最优；GPT-OSS 20B 在开源模型中表现领先。结构化领域（如电子、体育）的共识较强，而生活方式类别（如服装、食品）的意见分歧较大。ScalingEval 为LLM作为评测者提供了一个可复现的基准和评估协议，并就规模化、可靠性以及模型家族权衡提供了可操作的指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型（LLM）在各种应用中日益普及，评估LLM作为“裁判”或“评测者”的能力变得至关重要，这关系到构建可扩展且值得信赖的评估流程。然而，现有的LLM评估方法往往缺乏规模化、可复现性和客观性，尤其是在没有大量人工标注的情况下。因此，研究LLM作为评测者的有效性和可靠性，并开发相应的评估基准和协议，具有重要的理论和实践意义。

Method: 本研究提出了ScalingEval，一个大规模的基准研究，系统性地比较了36种不同的LLM，包括GPT、Gemini、Claude和Llama系列模型。评估协议采用了“共识驱动”的方法。具体来说，研究设计了一个多智能体框架，该框架能够对LLM的输出进行模式审计和问题编码，并通过大规模的多数投票机制将这些信息聚合，最终生成“事实标签”（ground-truth labels）。这种方法使得在不依赖人工标注的情况下，能够对LLM作为评测者的能力进行可复现的比较。该基准被应用于大规模的互补品推荐场景，以验证其有效性。

Result: 在应用于大规模互补品推荐场景后，ScalingEval基准研究报告了四项关键发现：（1）Anthropic Claude 3.5 Sonnet 在评估任务中展现了最高的决策置信度。（2）Gemini 1.5 Pro 在跨越多个产品类别进行综合评估时，表现最为全面和优异。（3）GPT-4o 在评估效率方面表现突出，提供了最佳的延迟-准确性-成本权衡。（4）在开源模型中，GPT-OSS 20B 取得了领先地位。此外，对不同产品类别的分析显示，在电子产品和体育用品等结构化领域，LLM评估者之间存在较强的共识；然而，在服装和食品等生活方式类别中，LLM评估者之间仍然存在持续的分歧。

Conclusion: ScalingEval的提出，为评估大型语言模型（LLM）作为“裁判”的能力提供了一个可复现的基准和评估协议。该研究通过大规模、多模型、多类别的系统性比较，不仅揭示了不同LLM在评估任务上的性能差异，例如Claude 3.5 Sonnet的置信度、Gemini 1.5 Pro的综合性能、GPT-4o的效率以及GPT-OSS 20B在开源模型中的优势，还指出了在不同类型数据上评估共识度的差异。这些发现为选择和优化LLM作为评估工具提供了可操作的指导，特别是在规模化、可靠性以及不同模型家族之间的权衡方面。未来的工作可以进一步扩展ScalingEval的覆盖范围，探索更多领域和模型，并深入研究导致生活方式类别评估分歧的原因。

Abstract: Evaluating large language models (LLMs) as judges is increasingly critical
for building scalable and trustworthy evaluation pipelines. We present
ScalingEval, a large-scale benchmarking study that systematically compares 36
LLMs, including GPT, Gemini, Claude, and Llama, across multiple product
categories using a consensus-driven evaluation protocol. Our multi-agent
framework aggregates pattern audits and issue codes into ground-truth labels
via scalable majority voting, enabling reproducible comparison of LLM
evaluators without human annotation. Applied to large-scale complementary-item
recommendation, the benchmark reports four key findings: (i) Anthropic Claude
3.5 Sonnet achieves the highest decision confidence; (ii) Gemini 1.5 Pro offers
the best overall performance across categories; (iii) GPT-4o provides the most
favorable latency-accuracy-cost tradeoff; and (iv) GPT-OSS 20B leads among
open-source models. Category-level analysis shows strong consensus in
structured domains (Electronics, Sports) but persistent disagreement in
lifestyle categories (Clothing, Food). These results establish ScalingEval as a
reproducible benchmark and evaluation protocol for LLMs as judges, with
actionable guidance on scaling, reliability, and model family tradeoffs.

</details>


### [69] [Epidemiology of Large Language Models: A Benchmark for Observational Distribution Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03070)
*Drago Plecko,Patrik Okanovic,Torsten Hoefler,Elias Bareinboim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个评估大型语言模型（LLM）在理解真实世界概率分布方面能力的基准。研究发现，LLM在处理概率知识方面表现不佳，未能自然地内化现实世界统计数据。这表明它们在因果层级中的观察层面上存在局限，进而限制了其干预和反事实推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着人工智能（AI）在科学和实际应用中的广泛应用，实现更通用的智能水平面临着知识表示的挑战。特别是在事实知识（可验证真伪）和概率知识（反映现实世界概率特性）之间存在关键区别。目前尚不清楚接受海量文本训练的大型语言模型（LLM）是否内化了现实世界的概率分布，尽管它们被认为是强大的通用分布逼近器。然而，统计学中的“维度灾难”理论对在高维空间中学习分布提出了根本性挑战。因此，本文旨在填补理解LLM概率知识能力的空白，并验证其作为通用分布学习者的能力。

Method: 本研究开发了一个直接测试LLM对现实世界概率分布理解能力的基准。该基准涵盖了经济学、健康、教育和社会行为等多个领域。通过设计一系列测试，评估LLM在多大程度上能够访问和理解描述真实世界人口的经验分布。研究重点在于衡量LLM对观察性分布（因果层级的第一层）的掌握程度。

Result: 研究结果表明，LLM在理解和表示真实世界概率分布方面整体表现不佳。它们似乎未能自然地内化现实世界的统计数据。具体而言，LLM在因果层级（PCH）的观察层面上（Layer 1）知识匮乏。

Conclusion: 本研究构建的基准揭示了大型语言模型在概率知识方面的显著局限性。研究结果表明，LLM缺乏对现实世界观察性分布的理解，这根据因果层级理论（PCH），意味着它们在更高级别的干预（Layer 2）和反事实（Layer 3）推理能力上也受到限制。这项工作强调了在开发更通用人工智能系统时，需要解决LLM在概率和因果推理方面的不足。未来的研究可以致力于改进LLM的架构或训练方法，以增强其处理概率和因 causal 知识的能力。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) systems hold great promise for advancing various
scientific disciplines, and are increasingly used in real-world applications.
Despite their remarkable progress, further capabilities are expected in order
to achieve more general types of intelligence. A critical distinction in this
context is between factual knowledge, which can be evaluated against true or
false answers (e.g., "what is the capital of England?"), and probabilistic
knowledge, reflecting probabilistic properties of the real world (e.g., "what
is the sex of a computer science graduate in the US?"). In this paper, our goal
is to build a benchmark for understanding the capabilities of LLMs in terms of
knowledge of probability distributions describing the real world. Given that
LLMs are trained on vast amounts of text, it may be plausible that they
internalize aspects of these distributions. Indeed, LLMs are touted as powerful
universal approximators of real-world distributions. At the same time,
classical results in statistics, known as curse of dimensionality, highlight
fundamental challenges in learning distributions in high dimensions,
challenging the notion of universal distributional learning. In this work, we
develop the first benchmark to directly test this hypothesis, evaluating
whether LLMs have access to empirical distributions describing real-world
populations across domains such as economics, health, education, and social
behavior. Our results demonstrate that LLMs perform poorly overall, and do not
seem to internalize real-world statistics naturally. When interpreted in the
context of Pearl's Causal Hierarchy (PCH), our benchmark demonstrates that
language models do not contain knowledge on observational distributions (Layer
1 of PCH), and thus the Causal Hierarchy Theorem implies that interventional
(Layer 2) and counterfactual (Layer 3) knowledge of these models is also
limited.

</details>


### [70] [SnapStream: Efficient Long Sequence Decoding on Dataflow Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03092)
*Jonathan Li,Nasim Farahini,Evgenii Iuliugin,Magnus Vesterlund,Christian Haggstrom,Guangtao Wang,Shubhangi Upasani,Ayush Sachdeva,Rui Li,Faline Fu,Chen Wu,Ayesha Siddiqua,John Long,Tuowen Zhao,Matheen Musaddiq,Hakan Zeffer,Yun Du,Mingran Wang,Qinghua Li,Bo Li,Urmish Thakker,Raghu Prabhakar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）的参数量和上下文长度不断增长，对片上内存提出了更高的要求，以支持巨大的 KV 缓存。虽然 StreamingLLM 和 SnapKV 等技术在控制 KV 缓存大小的同时保持模型准确性方面显示了潜力，但由于现有框架（如 vLLM 和 SGLang）的静态图和连续批处理方法难以集成这些技术，并且对现代模型的影响尚不明确，因此它们并未在工业部署中广泛应用。本文提出了 SnapStream，一种可大规模部署的 KV 缓存压缩方法，该方法在 Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct 和 DeepSeek-R1 模型上进行了准确性分析，并在 16 路张量并行部署的 DeepSeek-671B 模型上进行了实际生产环境验证。SnapStream 在 128k 上下文长度和高达 1832 token/秒的吞吐量下，实现了 4 倍的片上内存使用率提升，并在 LongBench-v2、AIME24 和 LiveCodeBench 基准测试中仅带来极小的准确性下降。这是首个在具有静态图和连续批处理的生产推理系统中实现的稀疏 KV 注意力技术实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 100B+ 参数和 100k+ 上下文长度的大型语言模型（LLMs）的出现，对片上内存（尤其是 KV 缓存）的需求急剧增加。现有的 KV 缓存优化技术（如 StreamingLLM 和 SnapKV）虽然在理论上有效，但在实际工业部署中面临两大挑战：1) 现有主流推理框架（如 vLLM, SGLang）的静态计算图和连续批处理机制难以集成这些优化技术；2) 这些技术对现代指令遵循和推理模型的准确性影响尚不明确，导致实施动力不足。因此，有必要研究这些技术对实际模型的影响，并开发一种能够克服现有框架限制、可大规模部署的 KV 缓存优化方案。

Method: 本文首先分析了 KV 缓存优化技术（如 StreamingLLM 和 SnapKV）在 Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct 和 DeepSeek-R1 模型上的准确性影响。基于这些分析，研究人员开发了一种名为 SnapStream 的新型 KV 缓存压缩方法。SnapStream 被设计成能够适应具有静态图和连续批处理的推理框架。为了验证 SnapStream 的有效性和可扩展性，研究人员在一个生产环境中进行了实验：使用 16 路张量并行技术部署 DeepSeek-671B 模型，在 SambaNova SN40L 加速器上运行，支持 128k 的上下文长度，并评估了其吞吐量和内存使用效率。同时，在 LongBench-v2、AIME24 和 LiveCodeBench 等基准测试上评估了 SnapStream 对模型准确性的影响。

Result: SnapStream 在实际生产环境中表现出色，在 16 路张量并行部署的 DeepSeek-671B 模型上，实现了高达 1832 tokens/秒的吞吐量，上下文长度达到 128k。与基线相比，SnapStream 能够实现 4 倍的片上内存使用率提升。在 LongBench-v2、AIME24 和 LiveCodeBench 等多个基准测试中，SnapStream 仅引入了极小的准确性下降。研究表明，SnapStream 是一种在保持高性能的同时有效管理 KV 缓存内存的解决方案。

Conclusion: 本文成功开发并验证了 SnapStream，一种可在生产推理系统中大规模部署的 KV 缓存压缩技术。SnapStream 克服了现有主流推理框架在集成 KV 缓存优化技术方面的限制，并在实际应用中实现了显著的内存效率提升（4 倍）和高吞吐量（1832 tokens/秒），同时对模型准确性造成的影响极小。这是首次在带有静态图和连续批处理的生产推理系统中成功部署稀疏 KV 注意力技术，为未来 LLMs 的高效部署提供了重要实践。未来的工作可以进一步探索 SnapStream 在更多模型和硬件平台上的适用性，以及更复杂的压缩策略。

Abstract: The proliferation of 100B+ parameter Large Language Models (LLMs) with 100k+
context length support have resulted in increasing demands for on-chip memory
to support large KV caches. Techniques such as StreamingLLM and SnapKV
demonstrate how to control KV cache size while maintaining model accuracy. Yet,
these techniques are not commonly used within industrial deployments using
frameworks like vLLM or SGLang. The reason is twofold: on one hand, the static
graphs and continuous batching methodology employed by these frameworks make it
difficult to admit modifications to the standard multi-head attention
algorithm, while on the other hand, the accuracy implications of such
techniques on modern instruction-following and reasoning models are not well
understood, obfuscating the need for implementing these techniques. In this
paper, we explore these accuracy implications on Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct and
DeepSeek-R1, and develop SnapStream, a KV cache compression method that can be
deployed at scale. We demonstrate the efficacy of SnapStream in a 16-way
tensor-parallel deployment of DeepSeek-671B on SambaNova SN40L accelerators
running at 128k context length and up to 1832 tokens per second in a real
production setting. SnapStream enables $4\times$ improved on-chip memory usage
and introduces minimal accuracy degradation on LongBench-v2, AIME24 and
LiveCodeBench. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first implementation
of sparse KV attention techniques deployed in a production inference system
with static graphs and continuous batching.

</details>


### [71] [Outbidding and Outbluffing Elite Humans: Mastering Liar's Poker via Self-Play and Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03724)
*Richard Dewey,Janos Botyanszki,Ciamac C. Moallemi,Andrew T. Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Solly是首个在多人、不完美信息游戏中达到精英人类水平的AI。该研究使用深度强化学习训练Solly，并在Liar's Poker游戏中取得了超过50%的胜率和高额回报，优于大型语言模型，并展现出新颖的策略。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用无模型、Actor-Critic深度强化学习算法，通过自我对弈的方式训练AI智能体Solly。实验在Liar's Poker（包括单挑和多人模式）中进行评估，并与世界级人类玩家及大型语言模型（LLMs）进行性能比较。

Abstract: AI researchers have long focused on poker-like games as a testbed for
environments characterized by multi-player dynamics, imperfect information, and
reasoning under uncertainty. While recent breakthroughs have matched elite
human play at no-limit Texas hold'em, the multi-player dynamics are subdued:
most hands converge quickly with only two players engaged through multiple
rounds of bidding. In this paper, we present Solly, the first AI agent to

by extensive multi-player engagement. We trained Solly using self-play with a
model-free, actor-critic, deep reinforcement learning algorithm. Solly played

randomized play effectively, and was not easily exploitable by world-class
human players.

### [72] [Large language models require a new form of oversight: capability-based monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03106)
*Katherine C. Kellogg,Bingyang Ye,Yifan Hu,Guergana K. Savova,Byron Wallace,Danielle S. Bitterman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 传统机器学习的监测方法在医疗领域的大型语言模型（LLM）上存在局限性，因为LLM是通用模型，不针对特定任务进行训练。本文提出了一种新的“能力导向监测”方法，围绕LLM的通用能力（如摘要、推理、翻译、安全护栏）进行监测，以跨任务检测系统性弱点、长尾错误和新兴行为，从而为LLM在医疗领域的安全、自适应和协作化监测奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM监测方法沿用传统机器学习的思路，基于假定因数据集漂移导致的性能下降。然而，LLM作为通用模型，其性能下降并非源于特定任务的数据集漂移，而是由于模型本身能力的退化。因此，需要一种新的监测原则来适应LLM的通用性和开发使用模式。

Method: 本文提出了一种“能力导向监测”的组织原则。该方法不单独评估每个下游任务，而是围绕LLM共享的通用能力（如摘要、推理、翻译、安全护栏）进行监测。通过关注这些核心能力，可以跨不同任务检测系统性弱点、长尾错误和新兴行为，这是基于任务的监测方法可能忽略的。

Result: 能力导向监测能够实现跨任务检测系统性弱点、长尾错误和新兴行为。该方法为LLM在医疗领域的安全、自适应和协作化监测提供了可扩展的基础。

Conclusion: 能力导向监测是一种比传统基于任务的监测方法更适合通用LLM的监测原则。它通过关注LLM的核心通用能力，实现了更全面、可扩展的监测，为LLM在医疗领域的安全应用提供了重要的支持。该方法为未来通用人工智能模型的监测提供了借鉴。

Abstract: The rapid adoption of large language models (LLMs) in healthcare has been
accompanied by scrutiny of their oversight. Existing monitoring approaches,
inherited from traditional machine learning (ML), are task-based and founded on
assumed performance degradation arising from dataset drift. In contrast, with
LLMs, inevitable model degradation due to changes in populations compared to
the training dataset cannot be assumed, because LLMs were not trained for any
specific task in any given population. We therefore propose a new organizing
principle guiding generalist LLM monitoring that is scalable and grounded in
how these models are developed and used in practice: capability-based
monitoring. Capability-based monitoring is motivated by the fact that LLMs are
generalist systems whose overlapping internal capabilities are reused across
numerous downstream tasks. Instead of evaluating each downstream task
independently, this approach organizes monitoring around shared model
capabilities, such as summarization, reasoning, translation, or safety
guardrails, in order to enable cross-task detection of systemic weaknesses,
long-tail errors, and emergent behaviors that task-based monitoring may miss.
We describe considerations for developers, organizational leaders, and
professional societies for implementing a capability-based monitoring approach.
Ultimately, capability-based monitoring will provide a scalable foundation for
safe, adaptive, and collaborative monitoring of LLMs and future generalist
artificial intelligence models in healthcare.

### [73] [miniF2F-Lean Revisited: Reviewing Limitations and Charting a Path Forward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03108)
*Azim Ospanov,Farzan Farnia,Roozbeh Yousefzadeh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究对 miniF2F 基准进行了详细分析，重点关注 AI 系统在数学奥林匹克竞赛中的应用。研究发现，当前的 AI 模型在理解、形式化和证明数学问题方面存在显著挑战，整体准确率仅为 36%，远低于单独的模型性能。分析显示，形式化陈述与非形式化陈述之间的不一致是导致准确率下降的主要原因。为解决此问题，研究提出了 miniF2F-v2 版本，修正了所有陈述中的错误和不一致，并提供了经过验证的证明。在 miniF2F-v2 上重新评估后，整体准确率提升至 70%，但仍表明自动形式化模型与定理证明器之间存在较大差距。研究强调了高质量基准测试对于评估和诊断形式化推理领域模型进展的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数学奥林匹克竞赛通常包含需要严谨证明的复杂问题。虽然 AI 在数学领域取得了显著进展，但在模拟 AI 参加此类竞赛时，仍面临巨大挑战。具体而言，AI 系统需要能够准确理解自然语言表述的问题，将其转化为形式化语言（如 Lean），并生成可靠的数学证明。然而，目前 AI 在这一整个流程中的表现并不理想，尤其是在形式化与非形式化陈述一致性方面存在问题，这严重影响了其在真实竞赛场景中的应用效果。因此，本研究旨在深入分析这些问题，并提出改进方案，以期更好地评估和提升 AI 在形式化推理方面的能力。

Method: 本研究首先对 miniF2F 基准进行了详细分析，模拟了一个 AI 系统参加数学奥林匹克竞赛的场景。该系统需要完成阅读理解、Lean 语言形式化以及定理证明等步骤。研究人员使用现有的最先进（SoTA）模型评估了这一完整流程的准确性，并将其与单个模型（如自动形式化模型和定理证明模型）的性能进行了比较。在分析失败模式后，研究人员发现形式化陈述与非形式化陈述之间的不一致是导致性能下降的关键因素。为了解决这个问题，研究团队修正了 miniF2F 中所有形式化和非形式化陈述中的错误、不一致和简化之处，创建了一个名为 miniF2F-v2 的新版本。最后，研究人员在改进后的 miniF2F-v2 基准上重新评估了整个定理证明流程，以量化改进效果并进一步诊断模型间的对齐问题。

Result: 研究结果表明，在原始 miniF2F 基准上，采用 SoTA 模型的完整 AI 证明流程的准确率仅为 36%，远低于自动形式化模型（97%）和定理证明模型（69%）各自的准确率。对失败模式的分析发现，超过一半的问题存在形式化与非形式化陈述不一致的情况，这是导致整体准确率显著下降的主要原因。在修正了这些不一致并推出 miniF2F-v2 版本后，完整流程的准确率提升至 70%。尽管这一改进是显著的，但相比于单独的定理证明器 69% 的准确率，70% 的提升仍然表明自动形式化模型在将非形式化陈述转化为形式化表示时，与定理证明器的目标仍存在较大差距。

Conclusion: 本研究通过对 miniF2F 基准的深入分析，揭示了当前 AI 系统在形式化推理，特别是模拟数学奥林匹克竞赛场景下面临的严峻挑战。研究发现，形式化陈述与非形式化陈述之间的一致性是影响整体性能的关键因素。通过创建和评估更正后的 miniF2F-v2 基准，研究不仅显著提升了 AI 证明流程的准确率，而且更清晰地暴露了自动形式化模型与定理证明器之间的对齐问题。研究强调，开发更高质量、更一致的基准测试对于准确评估形式化推理领域的进展至关重要，并有助于更精确地诊断模型在形式化和证明过程中遇到的成功与失败模式。未来的工作可以集中于改进自动形式化模型，使其生成的陈述与定理证明器的要求更加匹配。

Abstract: We perform a thorough analysis of the formal and informal statements in the
miniF2F benchmark from the perspective of an AI system that is tasked to
participate in a math Olympiad consisting of the problems in miniF2F. In such
setting, the model has to read and comprehend the problems in natural language,
formalize them in Lean language, then proceed with proving the problems, and it
will get credit for each problem if the formal proof corresponds to the
original informal statement presented to the model. Our evaluation results
reveal that the best accuracy of such pipeline can be about 36% using the SoTA
models in the literature, considerably lower than the individual SoTA
accuracies, 97% and 69% reported in the autoformalization and theorem proving
literature. Analyzing the failure modes, we trace back a considerable portion
of this drop to discrepancies between the formal and informal statements for
more than half of the problems in miniF2F. We proceed with correcting all the
errors, discrepancies and simplifications in formal and informal statements,
and present the miniF2F-v2 with fully verified formal and informal statements
and proofs. Evaluating the full theorem proving pipeline on miniF2F-v2 leads to
the best accuracy of 70%, a significant improvement from the 40% on the
original miniF2F, yet indicating considerable misalignment between the
autoformalization models and theorem provers. Our deep analysis suggests that a
higher quality benchmark can help the community better evaluate progress in the
field of formal reasoning and also better diagnose the failure and success
modes of autoformalization and theorem proving models. Our dataset is available
at https://github.com/roozbeh-yz/miniF2F_v2.

</details>


### [74] [Beyond Single Pass, Looping Through Time: KG-IRAG with Iterative Knowledge Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2503.14234)
*Ruiyi Yang,Hao Xue,Imran Razzak,Hakim Hacid,Flora D. Salim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 图谱检索增强生成（GraphRAG）通过利用知识图谱（KGs）提高了大语言模型（LLMs）在需要外部知识的任务中的表现。然而，大多数RAG方法难以处理需要信息抽取和推理的多步推理任务。本文提出的知识图谱驱动的迭代检索增强生成（KG-IRAG）框架，通过结合知识图谱和迭代推理，解决了这一局限性。KG-IRAG通过迭代检索逐步收集外部知识图谱中的相关数据，从而实现逐步推理，特别适用于需要动态时间数据抽取和推理的场景，例如基于天气或交通状况确定最佳出行时间。实验结果表明，KG-IRAG通过有效整合外部知识和迭代的、基于逻辑的检索，提高了复杂推理任务的准确性。此外，本文还构建了三个新的数据集（weatherQA-Irish、weatherQA-Sydney和trafficQA-TFNSW）来评估KG-IRAG的性能，证明了其在传统RAG应用之外的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的检索增强生成（RAG）方法在处理需要多步推理的任务时存在不足，特别是在需要信息抽取和推理的情况下。这些方法难以有效处理涉及时间依赖性和逻辑推理的复杂查询。因此，有必要开发一种新的框架来增强LLMs在处理此类复杂推理任务方面的能力，尤其是在需要动态时间数据抽取和推理的场景中。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为知识图谱驱动的迭代检索增强生成（KG-IRAG）的新框架。该框架将知识图谱（KGs）与迭代推理相结合，以增强大语言模型（LLMs）处理涉及时间依赖性和逻辑推理的查询的能力。KG-IRAG通过多步迭代检索过程，逐步从外部知识图谱中收集相关信息，从而实现逐步推理。此外，研究人员还构建了weatherQA-Irish、weatherQA-Sydney和trafficQA-TFNSW三个新的数据集，用于评估KG-IRAG的性能。

Result: 实验结果表明，KG-IRAG在复杂推理任务中显著提高了准确性。通过有效地整合外部知识和采用迭代的、基于逻辑的检索方法，KG-IRAG能够更好地处理需要多步推理和动态时间数据抽取的问题。在所构建的三个新数据集上的评估也证明了KG-IRAG的有效性，表明其性能超越了传统的RAG应用。

Conclusion: 本文提出的KG-IRAG框架通过结合知识图谱和迭代推理，有效地解决了现有RAG方法在处理多步复杂推理任务方面的局限性。该方法通过迭代检索逐步收集信息，实现了逐步推理，尤其适用于涉及动态时间数据和逻辑依赖的场景。实验结果和新数据集的构建证明了KG-IRAG在提高LLM推理能力方面的潜力，为未来在需要复杂知识整合和推理的应用领域开辟了新的可能性。

Abstract: Graph Retrieval-Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) has proven highly effective
in enhancing the performance of Large Language Models (LLMs) on tasks that
require external knowledge. By leveraging Knowledge Graphs (KGs), GraphRAG
improves information retrieval for complex reasoning tasks, providing more
precise and comprehensive retrieval and generating more accurate responses to
QAs. However, most RAG methods fall short in addressing multi-step reasoning,
particularly when both information extraction and inference are necessary. To
address this limitation, this paper presents Knowledge Graph-Based Iterative
Retrieval-Augmented Generation (KG-IRAG), a novel framework that integrates KGs
with iterative reasoning to improve LLMs' ability to handle queries involving
temporal and logical dependencies. Through iterative retrieval steps, KG-IRAG
incrementally gathers relevant data from external KGs, enabling step-by-step
reasoning. The proposed approach is particularly suited for scenarios where
reasoning is required alongside dynamic temporal data extraction, such as
determining optimal travel times based on weather conditions or traffic
patterns. Experimental results show that KG-IRAG improves accuracy in complex
reasoning tasks by effectively integrating external knowledge with iterative,
logic-based retrieval. Additionally, three new datasets: weatherQA-Irish,
weatherQA-Sydney, and trafficQA-TFNSW, are formed to evaluate KG-IRAG's
performance, demonstrating its potential beyond traditional RAG applications.

</details>


### [75] [Using Multi-modal Large Language Model to Boost Fireworks Algorithm's Ability in Settling Challenging Optimization Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03137)
*Shipeng Cen,Ying Tan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用多模态大语言模型（MLLM）辅助设计烟花算法（FWA）的新方法，以应对复杂高维优化问题的挑战。通过引入“关键部分”（CP）的概念并利用MLLM的多模态能力，优化后的FWA在旅行商问题（TSP）和电子设计自动化（EDA）问题上取得了与当前最优（SOTA）相当甚至更优的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着优化问题日益复杂和多样化，传统的优化技术在处理非凸性、高维度、黑盒等挑战时效率低下且梯度信息不准确。大型语言模型（LLM）在语言理解和代码生成方面的快速发展，为优化算法的设计带来了新的机遇。本研究旨在克服传统优化方法在处理复杂优化问题时的局限性，并探索利用MLLM提升优化算法性能的可能性。

Method: 本研究选择了烟花算法（FWA）作为基础优化器，并提出了一种新颖的辅助设计方法，该方法结合了多模态大语言模型（MLLM）。核心创新在于提出了“关键部分”（CP）的概念，旨在将FWA扩展到处理复杂的高维任务。此外，研究利用MLLM的多模态特性来更好地利用优化过程中的信息。实验主要针对旅行商问题（TSP）和电子设计自动化（EDA）问题进行。
