Conclusion: 本研究成功地展示了利用多模态大语言模型（MLLM）来改进烟花算法（FWA）的可行性，并通过“关键部分”（CP）的概念有效解决了复杂高维优化问题。实验结果证明了该方法的优越性，为未来结合AI大模型与优化算法的研究提供了有价值的参考。未来的工作可以探索将此方法应用于更广泛的优化领域，并进一步优化MLLM在优化过程中的作用。

Abstract: As optimization problems grow increasingly complex and diverse, advancements
in optimization techniques and paradigm innovations hold significant
importance. The challenges posed by optimization problems are primarily
manifested in their non-convexity, high-dimensionality, black-box nature, and
other unfavorable characteristics. Traditional zero-order or first-order
methods, which are often characterized by low efficiency, inaccurate gradient
information, and insufficient utilization of optimization information, are
ill-equipped to address these challenges effectively. In recent years, the
rapid development of large language models (LLM) has led to substantial
improvements in their language understanding and code generation capabilities.
Consequently, the design of optimization algorithms leveraging large language
models has garnered increasing attention from researchers. In this study, we
choose the fireworks algorithm(FWA) as the basic optimizer and propose a novel
approach to assist the design of the FWA by incorporating multi-modal large
language model(MLLM). To put it simply, we propose the concept of Critical
Part(CP), which extends FWA to complex high-dimensional tasks, and further
utilizes the information in the optimization process with the help of the
multi-modal characteristics of large language models. We focus on two specific
tasks: the \textit{traveling salesman problem }(TSP) and \textit{electronic
design automation problem} (EDA). The experimental results show that FWAs
generated under our new framework have achieved or surpassed SOTA results on
many problem instances.

### [76] [A Proprietary Model-Based Safety Response Framework for AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03138)
*Qi Li,Jianjun Xu,Pingtao Wei,Jiu Li,Peiqiang Zhao,Jiwei Shi,Xuan Zhang,Yanhui Yang,Xiaodong Hui,Peng Xu,Wenqin Shao*

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种新颖的安全响应框架，用于在输入和输出层面系统性地保护大型语言模型（LLMs），以解决LLMs日益突出的安全问题。该框架在输入层面使用监督微调的分类模型，采用细粒度的四级分类（安全、不安全、有条件安全、重点关注），实现了99.3%的风险召回率。在输出层面，结合检索增强生成（RAG）和一个专门的解释模型，确保响应基于可信知识库，消除信息捏造并实现结果可追溯。实验证明，该框架在公共安全评估基准和专有高风险测试集上均显著优于基线模型TinyR1-Safety-8B，在专有测试集上达到了100%的安全分数，为构建高安全性、高可信度的LLM应用提供了有效的工程途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）的广泛应用带来了日益严峻的安全问题，严重制约了其在关键领域的可靠部署。因此，研究如何有效保障LLMs的安全，防止其被滥用或产生不可信的输出，具有重要的现实意义和迫切的需求。

Method: 该研究提出了一种新颖的安全响应框架，该框架在输入和输出两个层面进行安全防护。在输入层面，采用监督微调（SFT）的分类模型，基于“安全、不安全、有条件安全、重点关注”的细粒度四级分类体系，对用户输入进行风险识别和区分处理。在输出层面，集成了检索增强生成（RAG）技术和一个经过专门微调的解释模型，确保LLM的响应内容基于实时、可信的知识库，从而消除信息虚构并实现结果的可追溯性。

Result: 实验结果表明，与基线模型TinyR1-Safety-8B相比，所提出的安全控制模型在公共安全评估基准上取得了显著更高的安全分数。在研究人员专有的高风险测试集上，该框架的各个组成部分均获得了100%的安全分数，证明了其在复杂风险场景下卓越的防护能力。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了一个在输入和输出层面均能有效保障LLM安全性的框架，通过精细化的风险分类和基于可信知识库的响应生成，显著提高了LLM的安全性与可信度。该框架在各项测试中均表现出色，尤其是在高风险场景下达到了完美的防护效果，为构建安全可靠的LLM应用提供了有效的工程化解决方案。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在更多样化、更复杂场景下的适应性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: With the widespread application of Large Language Models (LLMs), their
associated security issues have become increasingly prominent, severely
constraining their trustworthy deployment in critical domains. This paper
proposes a novel safety response framework designed to systematically safeguard
LLMs at both the input and output levels. At the input level, the framework
employs a supervised fine-tuning-based safety classification model. Through a
fine-grained four-tier taxonomy (Safe, Unsafe, Conditionally Safe, Focused
Attention), it performs precise risk identification and differentiated handling
of user queries, significantly enhancing risk coverage and business scenario
adaptability, and achieving a risk recall rate of 99.3%. At the output level,
the framework integrates Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) with a
specifically fine-tuned interpretation model, ensuring all responses are
grounded in a real-time, trustworthy knowledge base. This approach eliminates
information fabrication and enables result traceability. Experimental results
demonstrate that our proposed safety control model achieves a significantly
higher safety score on public safety evaluation benchmarks compared to the
baseline model, TinyR1-Safety-8B. Furthermore, on our proprietary high-risk
test set, the framework's components attained a perfect 100% safety score,
validating their exceptional protective capabilities in complex risk scenarios.
This research provides an effective engineering pathway for building
high-security, high-trust LLM applications.

Abstract: The exponential growth of Low Earth Orbit (LEO) satellites has revolutionised
Earth Observation (EO) missions, addressing challenges in climate monitoring,
disaster management, and more. However, autonomous coordination in
multi-satellite systems remains a fundamental challenge. Traditional
optimisation approaches struggle to handle the real-time decision-making
demands of dynamic EO missions, necessitating the use of Reinforcement Learning
(RL) and Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL). In this paper, we
investigate RL-based autonomous EO mission planning by modelling
single-satellite operations and extending to multi-satellite constellations
using MARL frameworks. We address key challenges, including energy and data
storage limitations, uncertainties in satellite observations, and the
complexities of decentralised coordination under partial observability. By
leveraging a near-realistic satellite simulation environment, we evaluate the
training stability and performance of state-of-the-art MARL algorithms,
including PPO, IPPO, MAPPO, and HAPPO. Our results demonstrate that MARL can

non-stationarity and reward interdependency in multi-satellite coordination.

learning in decentralised EO missions.

### [80] [From Five Dimensions to Many: Large Language Models as Precise and Interpretable Psychological Profilers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03235)
*Yi-Fei Liu,Yi-Long Lu,Di He,Hang Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）可以通过分析少量人类心理测量数据（如“大五”人格量表）来准确预测其他心理特征。LLMs采用两阶段推理过程：首先将原始数据转化为自然语言的性格摘要，然后基于此摘要生成其他量表的回答。这种方法在捕捉人类心理结构方面表现出色，相关性分析的 $R^2$ 值超过0.89，优于仅基于语义相似性的预测，并接近于直接在数据集上训练的机器学习模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索大型语言模型（LLMs）在多大程度上能够从有限的定量心理学数据中，模拟和理解个体心理特征之间的相互关系。研究关注LLMs是否能通过“零样本”（zero-shot）学习的方式，有效捕捉人类心理结构的复杂性，并提供一种新的心理模拟和分析工具。

Method: 研究者向多种LLMs提供了816名个体的“大五”人格量表（Big Five Personality Scale）的回答。随后，要求LLMs扮演这些个体，并根据这些“大五”人格特质，模拟回答九种其他心理量表的问题。通过比较LLMs生成的回答与真实人类数据在量表间相关性模式上的匹配程度，来评估LLMs的性能。研究还分析了LLMs的推理过程，揭示了其将原始数据转化为自然语言摘要，再基于摘要进行预测的两阶段过程。

Result: LLMs在模拟人类心理结构方面表现出显著的准确性，其生成回答与真实人类数据在量表间相关性模式上的匹配度（$R^2 > 0.89$）非常高。这种“零样本”的预测性能明显优于仅依赖于语义相似性的基线模型，并且接近于直接使用特定数据集训练的机器学习模型。对LLMs推理过程的分析表明，它们能够通过信息选择和压缩，将“大五”人格特质转化为自然语言的性格摘要，并利用这些摘要进行推理。这些摘要不仅包含原始信息，还能捕捉到更深层次的、关于特质相互作用的涌现模式，甚至可以提升预测的准确性。

Conclusion: 研究证明，LLMs能够通过高度抽象和推理的能力，从极少量的数据中精确预测个体的心理特征。这种能力为心理学模拟提供了强大的新工具，并揭示了LLMs在理解和生成复杂人类心理结构方面的潜力。研究结果表明，LLMs的推理过程并非简单的模式匹配，而是包含了一定程度的理解和概括能力。未来可进一步探索LLMs在心理学研究中的应用，以及优化其在特质重要性区分等方面的能力。

Abstract: Psychological constructs within individuals are widely believed to be
interconnected. We investigated whether and how Large Language Models (LLMs)
can model the correlational structure of human psychological traits from
minimal quantitative inputs. We prompted various LLMs with Big Five Personality
Scale responses from 816 human individuals to role-play their responses on nine
other psychological scales. LLMs demonstrated remarkable accuracy in capturing
human psychological structure, with the inter-scale correlation patterns from
LLM-generated responses strongly aligning with those from human data $(R^2 >
0.89)$. This zero-shot performance substantially exceeded predictions based on
semantic similarity and approached the accuracy of machine learning algorithms
trained directly on the dataset. Analysis of reasoning traces revealed that
LLMs use a systematic two-stage process: First, they transform raw Big Five
responses into natural language personality summaries through information
selection and compression, analogous to generating sufficient statistics.
Second, they generate target scale responses based on reasoning from these
summaries. For information selection, LLMs identify the same key personality
factors as trained algorithms, though they fail to differentiate item
importance within factors. The resulting compressed summaries are not merely
redundant representations but capture synergistic information--adding them to
original scores enhances prediction alignment, suggesting they encode emergent,
second-order patterns of trait interplay. Our findings demonstrate that LLMs
can precisely predict individual participants' psychological traits from
minimal data through a process of abstraction and reasoning, offering both a
powerful tool for psychological simulation and valuable insights into their
emergent reasoning capabilities.

</details>

Conclusion: AAA框架通过人机协作和创新的AI技术（GRASP和MaC），有效解决了网页可访问性审计规模化和资源密集的问题，实现了端到端的自动化审计，并赋能审计人员。研究证明了AI在提升网页可访问性方面的潜力，并为未来的相关研究提供了新的数据集和见解，特别是关于小型语言模型在特定领域的适用性。

### [83] [Meta-Semantics Augmented Few-Shot Relational Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.05684)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: PromptMeta框架包含两个核心创新：1. 元语义提示（MSP）池：学习并整合跨任务共享的高层元语义，以支持新关系的知识迁移和适应。2. 可学习的融合机制：动态地将元语义与特定任务的关系信息结合起来，以适应不同的小样本任务。这两个组件都在元学习框架内与模型参数联合优化。

Result: 在两个真实世界的知识图谱基准上的广泛实验和分析表明，PromptMeta在有限监督的情况下，能够有效地适应新关系，验证了该方法的有效性。

Abstract: Few-shot relational learning on knowledge graph (KGs) aims to perform
reasoning over relations with only a few training examples. While current

seamlessly integrates meta-semantics with relational information for few-shot

meta-semantics shared across tasks, enabling effective knowledge transfer and
adaptation to newly emerging relations; and (2) a learnable fusion mechanism
that dynamically combines meta-semantics with task-specific relational
information tailored to different few-shot tasks. Both components are optimized
jointly with model parameters within a meta-learning framework. Extensive

### [84] [s3: You Don't Need That Much Data to Train a Search Agent via RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.14146)
*Pengcheng Jiang,Xueqiang Xu,Jiacheng Lin,Jinfeng Xiao,Zifeng Wang,Jimeng Sun,Jiawei Han*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: s3是一个轻量级、模型无关的框架，通过在生成准确性方面进行优化来改进检索增强生成（RAG）系统。它将检索器与生成器分离，使用“超越RAG的收益”作为奖励信号，仅需少量训练数据就能超越现有基线，并在多个问答基准测试中展现出更强的下游性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索增强生成（RAG）系统在利用外部知识时存在局限性：1. 仅使用不考虑下游效用的搜索指标（如NDCG）优化检索。2. 整个大型语言模型（LLM）进行联合微调，导致检索与生成耦合，限制了实际搜索效用，并且不兼容冻结或专有模型。

Method: 提出s3框架，该框架将检索器与生成器解耦。s3训练检索器使用“超越RAG的收益”（即相对于朴素RAG在生成准确性上的提升）作为奖励信号。该框架轻量级且模型无关。

Result: s3仅需2.4k训练样本，其性能就超过了在多达70倍以上数据上训练的基线模型。在六个通用问答和五个医学问答基准测试中，s3持续展现出更强的下游性能。

Conclusion: s3通过解耦检索器和生成器，并引入“超越RAG的收益”作为奖励，成功地优化了RAG系统的检索能力。该方法轻量级、模型无关，并且仅需少量数据即可取得显著效果，证明了其在提高检索效用和兼容性方面的潜力。未来的工作可以探索更广泛的应用场景和更复杂的检索任务。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems empower large language models
(LLMs) to access external knowledge during inference. Recent advances have
enabled LLMs to act as search agents via reinforcement learning (RL), improving
information acquisition through multi-turn interactions with retrieval engines.
However, existing approaches either optimize retrieval using search-only
metrics (e.g., NDCG) that ignore downstream utility or fine-tune the entire LLM
to jointly reason and retrieve-entangling retrieval with generation and
limiting the real search utility and compatibility with frozen or proprietary
models. In this work, we propose s3, a lightweight, model-agnostic framework
that decouples the searcher from the generator and trains the searcher using a
Gain Beyond RAG reward: the improvement in generation accuracy over naive RAG.
s3 requires only 2.4k training samples to outperform baselines trained on over
70x more data, consistently delivering stronger downstream performance across
six general QA and five medical QA benchmarks.

### [85] [LLM-Driven Collaborative Model for Untangling Commits via Explicit and Implicit Dependency Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16395)
*Bo Hou,Xin Tan,Kai Zheng,Fang Liu,Yinghao Zhu,Li Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 软件开发中，原子提交（Atomic commits）是最佳实践，但实际开发中常出现混合了不相关变更的“纠缠提交”（tangled commits），增加了代码审查和维护的难度。现有方法（如基于规则、特征或图）依赖浅层信号，难以区分显式依赖（如控制/数据流）和隐式依赖（如语义/概念关系）。本文提出 ColaUntangle，一个协同咨询框架，用于提交的解缠，它能同时建模显式和隐式依赖。ColaUntangle 采用多智能体架构，集成 LLM 驱动的智能体：一个专注于显式依赖，一个专注于隐式依赖，还有一个审查智能体通过迭代咨询综合它们的观点。为捕获结构和上下文信息，框架构建了显式和隐式上下文，使智能体能够以符号和语义深度进行代码关系推理。在 C# (1,612 个) 和 Java (14k 个) 数据集上评估表明，ColaUntangle 优于最佳基线，分别提高了 44% 和 82%。结果证明了 LLM 驱动的协同框架在自动化提交解缠方面的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际软件开发中，开发者经常提交包含多个不相关代码变更的“纠缠提交”，这使得代码审查、问题追踪和代码维护变得更加困难和低效。尽管已有一些方法尝试解决这个问题，但它们通常依赖于浅层的代码信号，难以有效地区分不同类型的依赖关系，特别是语义或概念上的隐式依赖，这限制了它们在复杂场景下的应用效果。因此，需要一种更有效的方法来自动区分和分离不同开发关注点的代码变更，以恢复提交的原子性，从而提高软件开发的质量和效率。

Method: 本文提出 ColaUntangle，一个利用大型语言模型（LLM）智能体协同工作的提交解缠框架。该框架包含三个核心智能体：1. 显式依赖智能体：专注于识别代码变更中的控制流和数据流等显式依赖关系。2. 隐式依赖智能体：专注于识别代码变更中的语义或概念上的隐式依赖关系。3. 审查智能体：负责综合前两个智能体的分析结果，并通过迭代咨询过程进行协调和优化。为了支持智能体的推理，框架构建了“显式上下文”和“隐式上下文”，以捕获代码的结构和语义信息。实验在两个数据集（1,612 个 C# 提交和 14,000 个 Java 提交）上进行了评估。

Result: ColaUntangle 在 C# 和 Java 数据集上的实验结果显示出显著的性能提升。与表现最佳的基线方法相比，ColaUntangle 在 C# 数据集上实现了 44% 的改进，在 Java 数据集上更是达到了 82% 的改进。这表明该框架能够更有效地识别和分离纠缠提交中的不同开发关注点。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 ColaUntangle 框架通过集成 LLM 驱动的协同智能体，成功地解决了软件开发中纠缠提交的问题。该框架能够同时处理显式和隐式依赖关系，并在两个大型数据集上取得了优于现有方法的显著性能提升。这证明了基于 LLM 的协同智能体架构在自动化代码分析任务（如提交解缠）中的巨大潜力。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在其他代码分析任务中的应用，以及优化智能体间的协作机制。

Abstract: Atomic commits, which address a single development concern, are a best
practice in software development. In practice, however, developers often
produce tangled commits that mix unrelated changes, complicating code review
and maintenance. Prior untangling approaches (rule-based, feature-based, or
graph-based) have made progress but typically rely on shallow signals and
struggle to distinguish explicit dependencies (e.g., control/data flow) from
implicit ones (e.g., semantic or conceptual relationships). In this paper, we
propose ColaUntangle, a new collaborative consultation framework for commit
untangling that models both explicit and implicit dependencies among code
changes. ColaUntangle integrates Large Language Model (LLM)-driven agents in a
multi-agent architecture: one agent specializes in explicit dependencies,
another in implicit ones, and a reviewer agent synthesizes their perspectives
through iterative consultation. To capture structural and contextual
information, we construct Explicit and Implicit Contexts, enabling agents to
reason over code relationships with both symbolic and semantic depth. We
evaluate ColaUntangle on two widely-used datasets (1,612 C# and 14k Java
tangled commits). Experimental results show that ColaUntangle outperforms the
best-performing baseline, achieving an improvement of 44% on the C# dataset and
82% on the Java dataset. These findings highlight the potential of LLM-based
collaborative frameworks for advancing automated commit untangling tasks.

### [86] [Data Dependency-Aware Code Generation from Enhanced UML Sequence Diagrams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.03379)
*Wenxin Mao,Zhitao Wang,Long Wang,Sirong Chen,Cuiyun Gao,Luyang Cao,Ziming Liu,Qiming Zhang,Jun Zhou,Zhi Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLMs在代码生成方面表现出色，但自然语言描述存在歧义，难以捕捉复杂需求。本文提出UML2Dep框架，利用增强的UML序列图和数据依赖推理（DDI）来解决此问题。增强的UML图包含决策表和API规范，明确了服务交互的结构关系和业务逻辑流。DDI任务通过形式化的约束数学推理，在代码生成前构建显式数据依赖图，提高了代码生成的准确性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的自然语言描述在生成代码时存在固有的歧义，难以准确表达复杂的系统需求，例如复杂的系统行为、条件逻辑、架构约束以及面向服务架构中的隐式数据依赖。这种歧义可能导致代码生成错误和效率低下。因此，需要一种能够消除歧义、明确捕捉复杂需求的方法来改进代码生成过程。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为UML2Dep的新型代码生成框架。该框架首先引入了增强的统一建模语言（UML）序列图，该图专门针对面向服务架构进行了优化，集成了决策表和API规范，明确了服务交互的结构关系和业务逻辑流，从而消除了语言歧义。其次，为了处理数据流的关键性，框架引入了专门的数据依赖推理（DDI）任务。DDI在实际代码合成之前，系统性地构建显式的数据依赖图。为了确保可靠性，DDI被形式化为一种约束数学推理任务，并采用了新颖的提示策略，以利用LLMs在数学推理方面的优势。此外，通过附加的静态解析和依赖剪枝，进一步降低了复杂规范的上下文复杂性和认知负担，从而提高了推理的准确性和效率。

Result: （论文摘要中未提供具体结果和性能指标，因此无法详细阐述）

Conclusion: UML2Dep框架通过结合增强的UML序列图和形式化的数据依赖推理（DDI）任务，有效解决了大型语言模型在代码生成中因自然语言描述的歧义而带来的挑战。该框架能够更精确地捕捉复杂需求，特别是面向服务架构中的数据依赖关系，从而提高代码生成的准确性和效率。虽然摘要中未提供具体实验结果，但其提出的方法论为解决代码生成领域的长期挑战提供了一个有前景的方向。未来的工作可以集中在通过大规模实验验证其性能，并探索其在更广泛应用场景下的适用性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) excel at generating code from natural language
(NL) descriptions. However, the plain textual descriptions are inherently
ambiguous and often fail to capture complex requirements like intricate system
behaviors, conditional logic, and architectural constraints; implicit data
dependencies in service-oriented architectures are difficult to infer and
handle correctly. To bridge this gap, we propose a novel step-by-step code
generation framework named UML2Dep by leveraging unambiguous formal
specifications of complex requirements. First, we introduce an enhanced Unified
Modeling Language (UML) sequence diagram tailored for service-oriented
architectures. This diagram extends traditional visual syntax by integrating
decision tables and API specifications, explicitly formalizing structural
relationships and business logic flows in service interactions to rigorously
eliminate linguistic ambiguity. Second, recognizing the critical role of data
flow, we introduce a dedicated data dependency inference (DDI) task. DDI
systematically constructs an explicit data dependency graph prior to actual
code synthesis. To ensure reliability, we formalize DDI as a constrained
mathematical reasoning task through novel prompting strategies, aligning with
LLMs' excellent mathematical strengths. Additional static parsing and
dependency pruning further reduce context complexity and cognitive load
associated with intricate specifications, thereby enhancing reasoning accuracy
and efficiency.

</details>


### [87] [ForTIFAI: Fending Off Recursive Training Induced Failure for AI Model Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.08972)
*Soheil Zibakhsh Shabgahi,Pedram Aghazadeh,Azalia Mirhoseini,Farinaz Koushanfar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 随着生成式AI模型对合成数据的依赖日益增加，模型崩溃（即模型性能随训练代数下降）成为一个严峻挑战。本研究提出了一种名为截断交叉熵（TCE）的新型损失函数，通过选择性忽略高置信度（高对数似然）的token来过滤掉机器生成的痕迹，从而有效缓解模型崩溃。实验表明，使用TCE训练的模型能够容忍多2.3倍的合成数据而不会发生崩溃，并且提供了一个开放的基准来研究混合数据环境下的崩溃动态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI模型训练日益依赖合成数据，但重复训练会导致模型崩溃，从而降低模型性能。现有缓解模型崩溃的策略有限，而模型崩溃对AI模型的长期有效性构成了重大威胁。

Method: 本研究提出了一种名为截断交叉熵（TCE）的损失函数。TCE的原理是利用自回归模型倾向于生成高置信度文本的特性，在训练过程中选择性地忽略高置信度token，从而过滤掉潜在的机器生成伪影。此外，研究还构建了一个用于评估混合数据环境下模型崩溃动力学的开源基准。

Result: 使用TCE训练的模型不仅学习效率高，而且在模型崩溃方面的鲁棒性显著增强，能够容忍多2.3倍的合成数据。研究结果表明，置信度感知训练目标能够有效延缓模型崩溃的发生，为在暴露于合成数据时提高模型鲁棒性提供了一种实用且通用的工具。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的TCE损失函数是一种有效缓解生成式AI模型因训练合成数据而导致模型崩溃的策略。通过置信度感知训练，TCE能够显著提高模型对合成数据的容忍度。研究还提供了一个开源基准，有助于进一步研究模型崩溃动力学。TCE提供了一种实用且通用的方法来增强模型在合成数据暴露下的鲁棒性，为应对未来数据环境中合成数据激增的挑战提供了关键解决方案。

Abstract: The increasing reliance on generative AI models is rapidly increasing the
volume of synthetic data, with some projections suggesting that most available
new data for training could be machine-generated by 2030. This shift to a
mainly synthetic content presents a critical challenge: repeated training in
synthetic data leads to a phenomenon known as model collapse, where model
performance degrades over generations of training, eventually rendering the
models ineffective. While the causes of model collapse are increasingly
understood, effective mitigation strategies remain scarce. We address this
challenge by leveraging a key insight: auto-regressive models tend to generate
text sequences to which they assign high confidence (i.e., high
log-likelihood). Based on this observation, we introduce the
Truncated-Cross-Entropy (TCE) loss function. TCE mitigates collapse by
selectively ignoring high-confidence tokens during training, effectively
filtering out likely machine-generated artifacts from the learning process. Our
experiments demonstrate that models trained with TCE not only learn effectively
but also exhibit significantly increased resilience, tolerating over 2.3x more
synthetic data before the onset of collapse. In addition, we provide an
open-source benchmark for collapse dynamics in mixed-data settings. Our results
demonstrate that confidence-aware training objectives can substantially delay
collapse onset, offering a practical and generalizable tool for model
robustness under synthetic-data exposure.

</details>


### [88] [VoiceAgentBench: Are Voice Assistants ready for agentic tasks?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.07978)
*Dhruv Jain,Harshit Shukla,Gautam Rajeev,Ashish Kulkarni,Chandra Khatri,Shubham Agarwal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 现有的语音语言模型（SpeechLMs）在理解自然语音查询和执行复杂任务方面取得了进展，但现有的语音基准测试未能系统地评估语音助手的多语言、文化理解能力以及对抗性鲁棒性等 agente 场景。为解决此问题，我们提出了 VoiceAgentBench，一个全面的基准测试，用于在真实的语音 agente 场景中评估 SpeechLMs。该基准包含超过 5,500 个合成语音查询，涵盖了单工具调用、多工具工作流、多轮交互和安全评估，并特别关注了印度本土的对话场景。它支持英语、印地语和另外 5 种印度语言，体现了真实的语言和文化多样性。我们通过一种新颖的采样算法来模拟说话人可变性，该算法根据说话人嵌入来选择用于 TTS 语音转换的音频，从而最大限度地提高声学和说话人多样性。评估指标包括工具选择准确性、结构一致性以及工具调用的正确性，并纳入了对抗性鲁棒性评估。实验结果表明，在上下文工具编排任务、印度语言泛化能力和对抗性鲁棒性方面存在显著的差距，暴露了当前 SpeechLMs 的关键局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语音基准测试主要侧重于语音识别或问答等孤立能力，未能全面评估语音语言模型（SpeechLMs）在实际应用场景中的 agente 能力，特别是在多语言、跨文化理解和对抗性鲁棒性方面。这阻碍了语音助手在复杂、多样化现实世界中的有效部署。因此，有必要开发一个能够系统性评估这些关键 agente 能力的综合基准。

Method: 我们提出了 VoiceAgentBench，一个包含超过 5,500 个合成语音查询的综合基准测试，用于评估 SpeechLMs 的 agente 能力。该基准包含了单工具调用、多工具工作流、多轮交互和安全评估等场景，并特别针对印度本土文化背景进行了设计。它支持英语、印地语和另外 5 种印度语言。为了模拟真实的说话人变化，我们采用了一种新颖的采样算法，基于说话人嵌入来选择用于文本到语音（TTS）语音转换的音频，以最大化声学和说话人多样性。评估指标包括工具选择准确性、结构一致性以及工具调用的正确性，并加入了对抗性鲁棒性测试。

Result: 我们的实验结果揭示了当前 SpeechLMs 在多个方面的显著局限性。在上下文工具编排任务中，模型在处理需要理解多轮对话和复杂依赖关系的任务时表现不佳。在印度语言泛化方面，模型在非英语语言上的性能明显下降，表明其跨语言和跨文化理解能力不足。此外，模型在对抗性鲁棒性测试中也表现脆弱，容易受到故意设计的扰动输入的影响。这些发现突显了现有 SpeechLMs 在实际应用中满足多样化需求方面的挑战。

Conclusion: VoiceAgentBench 的推出填补了现有语音基准测试在评估 SpeechLMsAgente 能力方面的空白，特别是在多语言、跨文化和鲁棒性方面。我们的研究揭示了当前 SpeechLMs 在这些关键领域存在的显著差距，为未来的研究提供了明确的方向。未来的工作可以集中于改进模型的上下文理解、多语言处理能力以及对抗性鲁棒性，以构建更强大、更可靠的语音助手。同时，可以进一步扩展基准测试，纳入更多样化的语言、文化背景和 agente 场景。

Abstract: Large-scale Speech Language Models (SpeechLMs) have enabled voice assistants
capable of understanding natural spoken queries and performing complex tasks.
However, existing speech benchmarks primarily focus on isolated capabilities
such as transcription, or question-answering, and do not systematically
evaluate agentic scenarios encompassing multilingual and cultural
understanding, as well as adversarial robustness. To address this, we introduce
VoiceAgentBench, a comprehensive benchmark designed to evaluate SpeechLMs in
realistic spoken agentic settings. It comprises over 5,500 synthetic spoken
queries, including dialogues grounded in Indian context, covering single-tool
invocations, multi-tool workflows, multi-turn interactions, and safety
evaluations. The benchmark supports English, Hindi, and 5 other Indian
languages, reflecting real-world linguistic and cultural diversity. We simulate
speaker variability using a novel sampling algorithm that selects audios for
TTS voice conversion based on its speaker embeddings, maximizing acoustic and
speaker diversity. Our evaluation measures tool selection accuracy, structural
consistency, and the correctness of tool invocations, including adversarial
robustness. Our experiments reveal significant gaps in contextual tool
orchestration tasks, Indic generalization, and adversarial robustness, exposing
critical limitations of current SpeechLMs.

</details>


### [89] [PlanU: Large Language Model Reasoning through Planning under Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.18442)
*Ziwei Deng,Mian Deng,Chenjing Liang,Zeming Gao,Chennan Ma,Chenxing Lin,Haipeng Zhang,Songzhu Mei,Siqi Shen,Cheng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理不确定性推理任务时面临挑战，尤其是在随机环境中进行规划。本文提出了一种名为PlanU的新方法，该方法将蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）与量分位数分布相结合，以捕捉环境和模型自身的不确定性。PlanU通过引入基于好奇心的上置信界（UCC）分数来平衡探索与利用，并在实验中证明了其在不确定性推理任务中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在各种推理任务中显示出潜力，但在处理人类相对容易的不确定性推理任务（如随机环境中的动作规划）时却遇到困难。这种不确定性主要源于LLM自身的随机采样过程（LLM不确定性）以及环境状态转换的随机性（环境不确定性）。现有的大多数基于LLM的决策（LDM）方法通过生成多个推理链或搜索树来解决LLM不确定性，但忽略了环境不确定性，导致在随机转换环境中性能下降。一些近期方法通过预测未知变量的概率来处理不确定性，但它们不适用于需要与环境交互的多步推理任务。因此，解决LLM在不确定性下的决策问题具有重要意义。

Method: 本文提出PlanU，一种基于LLM的规划方法，将不确定性纳入蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）。PlanU将MCTS中每个节点的返回值建模为量分位数分布，即使用一组分位数来表示返回值的分布。为了在树搜索中平衡探索与利用，PlanU引入了上置信界（UCC）分数，该分数估计MCTS节点的（不确定性）价值。

Result: 通过广泛的实验，我们证明了PlanU在LLM不确定性推理任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: PlanU通过将量分位数分布和UCC分数集成到MCTS中，成功地解决了LLM在不确定性环境下的决策规划问题，并在实验中取得了优于现有方法的性能。该方法为LLM在复杂、不确定环境中的应用提供了新的途径。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的环境模型和更精细的不确定性量化方法。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly being explored across a range
of reasoning tasks. However, LLMs sometimes struggle with reasoning tasks under
uncertainty that are relatively easy for humans, such as planning actions in
stochastic environments. The adoption of LLMs for reasoning is impeded by
uncertainty challenges, such as LLM uncertainty and environmental uncertainty.
LLM uncertainty arises from the stochastic sampling process inherent to LLMs.
Most LLM-based Decision-Making (LDM) approaches address LLM uncertainty through
multiple reasoning chains or search trees. However, these approaches overlook
environmental uncertainty, which leads to poor performance in environments with
stochastic state transitions. Some recent LDM approaches deal with uncertainty
by forecasting the probability of unknown variables. However, they are not
designed for multi-step reasoning tasks that require interaction with the
environment. To address uncertainty in LLM decision-making, we introduce PlanU,
an LLM-based planning method that captures uncertainty within Monte Carlo Tree
Search (MCTS). PlanU models the return of each node in the MCTS as a quantile
distribution, which uses a set of quantiles to represent the return
distribution. To balance exploration and exploitation during tree search, PlanU
introduces an Upper Confidence Bounds with Curiosity (UCC) score which
estimates the uncertainty of MCTS nodes. Through extensive experiments, we
demonstrate the effectiveness of PlanU in LLM-based reasoning tasks under
uncertainty.

</details>


### [90] [Agentic Meta-Orchestrator for Multi-task Copilots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22781)
*Xiaofeng Zhu,Yunshen Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Microsoft Copilot是一个通用的入口点，用于处理各种任务，如协助客户购买产品和检测代码漏洞。本文提出了一个Agentic Meta-orchestrator（AMO）来处理多任务和可扩展的智能体，该智能体利用元学习进行规划，并通过Microsoft 365电子商务Copilot和代码合规性Copilot进行了演示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着Copilot服务中智能体数量的增加，需要一个强大的协调器来将用户提示分配给正确的智能体，以处理从产品购买到代码安全等各种任务。

Method: 本文提出了Agentic Meta-orchestrator（AMO），一个用于处理多任务和可扩展智能体的系统。AMO利用元学习，具体来说是一个训练好的决策树模型，来决定各种智能体/模型之间的最佳推理策略。它能够提供自然语言和动作响应。

Result: AMO通过在Microsoft 365（M365）电子商务Copilot和代码合规性Copilot这两个生产用例中的有效性得到了展示。M365电子商务Copilot通过提供最新的产品信息并连接到关系数据库和人工客户支持等多个智能体来促进销售。代码合规性Copilot扫描内部DevOps代码，以检测拉取请求（PR）中已知和新的合规性问题。

Conclusion: AMO能够有效地处理多任务和可扩展的智能体，并在Microsoft 365电子商务和代码合规性Copilot等生产环境中得到证明。它通过利用元学习进行规划，并提供自然语言和动作响应，从而提高了Copilot服务的效率和能力。

Abstract: Microsoft Copilot suites serve as the universal entry point for various
agents skilled in handling important tasks, ranging from assisting a customer
with product purchases to detecting vulnerabilities in corporate programming
code. Each agent can be powered by language models, software engineering
operations, such as database retrieval, and internal \& external knowledge. The
repertoire of a copilot can expand dynamically with new agents. This requires a
robust orchestrator that can distribute tasks from user prompts to the right
agents. In this work, we propose an Agentic Meta-orchestrator (AMO) for
handling multiple tasks and scalable agents in copilot services, which can
provide both natural language and action responses. We will also demonstrate
the planning that leverages meta-learning, i.e., a trained decision tree model
for deciding the best inference strategy among various agents/models. We
showcase the effectiveness of our AMO through two production use cases:
Microsoft 365 (M365) E-Commerce Copilot and code compliance copilot. M365
E-Commerce Copilot advertises Microsoft products to external customers to
promote sales success. The M365 E-Commerce Copilot provides up-to-date product
information and connects to multiple agents, such as relational databases and
human customer support. The code compliance copilot scans the internal DevOps
code to detect known and new compliance issues in pull requests (PR).

</details>

### [91] [A Conditional Diffusion Model for Building Energy Modeling Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02930)
*Saumya Sinha,Alexandre Cortiella,Rawad El Kontar,Andrew Glaws,Ryan King,Patrick Emami*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用生成模型（特别是基于扩散的框架）来生成住宅楼宇的详细属性，以解决城市能源模型中数据缺失问题的创新方法。通过对220万栋建筑的大规模数据集进行训练，该模型能够生成逼真的建筑属性，从而填补数据空白，为能源模型提供更完整的输入。研究验证了该方法在生成条件分布和实际应用中的有效性，并展示了其在加速建筑能源建模工作流程方面的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前社区能源消耗行为的理解对于指导未来的能源使用决策和实现高效的能源管理至关重要。用于模拟这些能源使用模式的城市能源模型需要详细的建筑特征的大型数据集才能获得准确的结果。然而，个体建筑层面的详细特征通常是未知的、获取成本高昂或不可用的，这阻碍了能源模型的准确性和应用。因此，研究的动机在于解决这一数据获取的瓶颈，为能源模型提供完整、准确的建筑特征输入。

Method: 本研究提出使用一种生成建模方法来生成逼真的建筑属性，以填补数据空白。具体而言，研究采用了基于扩散的表格框架，该框架能够处理表格建筑数据中的异构特征（离散和连续），例如入住率、楼板面积、供暖、制冷和其他设备细节。研究开发了一种条件扩散能力，能够根据已知的属性推断缺失的建筑特征。模型在一个包含220万栋建筑的大规模住宅建筑存量模型上进行训练，以学习复杂的建筑层面的模式。

Result: 研究通过两种方式对条件扩散模型进行了全面验证。首先，通过比较生成条件分布与底层数据分布，评估了模型的拟合优度。其次，通过对巴尔的摩的一个住宅区域进行案例研究，展示了该方法的实际应用价值。结果表明，该方法能够生成与真实数据分布相似的建筑属性，并能有效地为能源模型提供完整输入。

Conclusion: 本研究是首次展示生成模型在加速建筑能源建模工作流程方面潜力的研究之一。通过使用条件扩散模型生成缺失的建筑属性，该研究有效地解决了城市能源模型在数据获取方面面临的挑战。该方法不仅能够生成逼真的建筑数据，还能根据已知信息进行推断，为能源建模提供了更准确、更全面的输入。这有望显著提高能源模型的精度和效率，并为社区能源管理提供有力支持。未来的工作可以进一步探索该模型在不同类型建筑和区域的应用，并与其他能源建模技术相结合。

Abstract: Understanding current energy consumption behavior in communities is critical
for informing future energy use decisions and enabling efficient energy
management. Urban energy models, which are used to simulate these energy use
patterns, require large datasets with detailed building characteristics for
accurate outcomes. However, such detailed characteristics at the individual
building level are often unknown and costly to acquire, or unavailable. Through
this work, we propose using a generative modeling approach to generate
realistic building attributes to fill in the data gaps and finally provide
complete characteristics as inputs to energy models. Our model learns complex,
building-level patterns from training on a large-scale residential building
stock model containing 2.2 million buildings. We employ a tabular
diffusion-based framework that is designed to handle heterogeneous (discrete
and continuous) features in tabular building data, such as occupancy, floor
area, heating, cooling, and other equipment details. We develop a capability
for conditional diffusion, enabling the imputation of missing building
characteristics conditioned on known attributes. We conduct a comprehensive
validation of our conditional diffusion model, firstly by comparing the
generated conditional distributions against the underlying data distribution,
and secondly, by performing a case study for a Baltimore residential region,
showing the practical utility of our approach. Our work is one of the first to
demonstrate the potential of generative modeling to accelerate building energy
modeling workflows.

</details>


### [92] [Simulation-Based Validation of an Integrated 4D/5D Digital-Twin Framework for Predictive Construction Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03684)
*Atena Khoshkonesh,Mohsen Mohammadagha,Navid Ebrahimi*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个集成了4D/5D数字孪生框架，结合了建筑信息模型（BIM）、自然语言处理（NLP）成本映射、计算机视觉（CV）进度测量、贝叶斯概率关键路径法（CPM）更新和深度强化学习（DRL）资源调平，以解决美国建筑行业成本和进度偏差的挑战。通过在达拉斯-沃斯堡的一个中层项目进行为期九个月的案例实施，该框架实现了估计劳动力减少43%、加班时间减少6%、项目缓冲区利用率30%，并保持了128天按时完工，置信度在P50-P80之间。数字孪生沙箱还通过5D知识图谱实现了实时的“what-if”预测和可追溯的成本-进度对齐。研究结果证实，将基于人工智能的分析与概率CPM和DRL相结合，能够提高预测的准确性、透明度和控制的韧性，为建立可预测、自适应和可审计的施工管理提供了实用的途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 美国建筑行业长期面临成本和进度偏差的严峻挑战，这暴露了传统确定性关键路径法（CPM）和基于静态文档的估算方法的局限性。这些挑战导致项目延误、成本超支，并损害了行业的整体效率和可靠性。因此，有必要开发更先进、更具适应性的方法来提高建筑项目的成本和进度预测的准确性与控制能力。

Method: 本研究提出并实施了一个集成的4D/5D数字孪生框架。该框架融合了多种先进技术：1）建筑信息模型（BIM）提供项目的三维几何和信息模型；2）基于自然语言处理（NLP）的成本映射技术，用于自动从文本描述中提取成本信息；3）计算机视觉（CV）驱动的进度测量，用于实时监控和量化现场施工进度；4）贝叶斯概率CPM更新，用于根据实际进度动态调整项目计划和风险评估；5）深度强化学习（DRL），用于优化资源分配和调度，实现有效的资源调平。研究在一个为期九个月的达拉斯-沃斯堡中层项目中进行了案例实施，以验证该框架的有效性。

Result: 在为期九个月的案例实施中，该集成框架取得了显著的成效：1）估算劳动力减少了43%；2）加班时间减少了6%；3）项目缓冲区（用于应对不确定性的缓冲时间）的利用率达到了30%。更重要的是，项目最终在128天内按时完工，并且其进度处于P50-P80的置信度范围内。此外，数字孪生沙箱能够支持实时的“what-if”情景分析，并通过5D知识图谱实现了成本和进度的高度可追溯性对齐。

Conclusion: 研究结果有力地证明，将人工智能（AI）驱动的分析（如NLP、CV和DRL）与概率CPM和BIM相结合，能够显著提升建筑项目成本和进度预测的准确性、过程的透明度以及管理的控制韧性。该经验证的工作流程为实现可预测、自适应和可审计的现代化施工管理提供了一条切实可行的路径，有望解决长期困扰建筑行业的成本和进度偏差问题。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在不同规模和类型项目中的应用，并持续优化AI算法以适应更复杂多变的施工环境。

Abstract: Persistent cost and schedule deviations remain a major challenge in the U.S.
construction industry, revealing the limitations of deterministic CPM and
static document-based estimating. This study presents an integrated 4D/5D
digital-twin framework that couples Building Information Modeling (BIM) with
natural-language processing (NLP)-based cost mapping, computer-vision
(CV)-driven progress measurement, Bayesian probabilistic CPM updating, and
deep-reinforcement-learning (DRL) resource-leveling. A nine-month case
implementation on a Dallas-Fort Worth mid-rise project demonstrated measurable
gains in accuracy and efficiency: 43% reduction in estimating labor, 6%
reduction in overtime, and 30% project-buffer utilization, while maintaining an
on-time finish at 128 days within P50-P80 confidence bounds. The digital-twin
sandbox also enabled real-time "what-if" forecasting and traceable
cost-schedule alignment through a 5D knowledge graph. Findings confirm that
integrating AI-based analytics with probabilistic CPM and DRL enhances
forecasting precision, transparency, and control resilience. The validated
workflow establishes a practical pathway toward predictive, adaptive, and
auditable construction management.

### [93] [ChemFM as a Scaling Law Guided Foundation Model Pre-trained on Informative Chemicals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2410.21422)
*Feiyang Cai,Katelin Zacour,Tianyu Zhu,Tzuen-Rong Tzeng,Yongping Duan,Ling Liu,Srikanth Pilla,Gang Li,Feng Luo*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: ChemFM是一个拥有30亿参数的化学领域基础模型，在1.78亿个分子上进行预训练，能够高效地适应各种下游化学任务，并在多项基准测试中超越了最先进的特定任务AI模型，尤其在性能提升、分子生成和反应预测方面表现突出，同时展示了强大的数据效率，有望推动化学研究和新药发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的AI方法在化学领域存在模型设计和训练的局限性，难以扩展模型规模和实现跨任务的泛化能力。这阻碍了AI在化学研究和药物发现等领域的广泛应用。

Method: 研究人员开发了一个名为ChemFM的大型基础模型，该模型拥有30亿参数。在预训练阶段，他们利用了UniChem数据库，并在1.78亿个分子上进行了自监督因果语言建模。训练完成后，ChemFM可以通过全参数微调或参数高效微调等方法来适应不同的下游化学应用。

Result: ChemFM在34个属性预测基准测试中，性能提升高达67.48%；在条件分子生成任务中，生成分子的实际属性与条件属性之间的平均偏差降低了33.80%；在4个反应预测数据集上，准确率提升了3.7%。此外，ChemFM在预测抗生素活性和细胞毒性方面也表现出色，并展示出强大的数据效率，以更少的数据样本达到最先进的性能。

Conclusion: ChemFM作为一个通用的化学基础模型，能够显著推进化学研究。它通过在广泛任务上实现有效的泛化能力，并需要最少的额外训练，有望加速新药的发现等应用。

Abstract: Traditional AI methods often rely on task-specific model designs and
training, which constrain both the scalability of model size and generalization
across different tasks. Here, we introduce ChemFM, a large foundation model
specifically developed for chemicals. By conducting a series of scaling
experiments, we identify UniChem as the informative molecular database for
pre-training the foundation model. ChemFM comprises 3 billion parameters and is
pre-trained on 178 million molecules using self-supervised causal language
modeling to extract generalizable molecular representations. This model can be
adapted to diverse downstream chemical applications using either full-parameter
or parameter-efficient fine-tuning methods. ChemFM consistently outperforms
state-of-the-art task-specific AI models across all tested tasks. Notably, it
achieves up to 67.48% performance improvement across 34 property prediction
benchmarks, up to 33.80% reduction in mean average deviation between
conditioned and actual properties of generated molecules in conditional
molecular generation tasks, and up to 3.7% top-1 accuracy improvement across 4
reaction prediction datasets. Moreover, ChemFM demonstrates its superior
performance in predicting antibiotic activity and cytotoxicity, highlighting
its potential to advance the discovery of novel antibiotics. Furthermore, we
demonstrate that, as a foundation model, ChemFM exhibits strong data
efficiency, requiring significantly fewer labeled training samples to achieve
state-of-the-art performance. We anticipate that ChemFM will significantly
advance chemistry research by providing a foundation model capable of
effectively generalizing across a broad range of tasks with minimal additional
training.

</details>


### [94] [A data-driven framework for team selection in Fantasy Premier League](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.02170)
*Danial Ramezani,Tai Dinh*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文研究了如何利用数据驱动的优化方法，结合历史数据和预测模型，来解决梦幻足球（Fantasy Premier League, FPL）中的阵容选择问题，旨在最大化未来积分。研究提出了确定性和鲁棒混合整数线性规划模型，考虑了预算、阵型和俱乐部球员数量限制。通过实验证明，ARIMA模型结合约束预算和滚动窗口的方法在样本外表现上最为稳定，其他方法如加权平均和蒙特卡洛模拟也具有竞争力。该框架为梦幻足球阵容构建提供了透明的决策支持，并可扩展至FPL的芯片使用、多周转会规划和动态队长选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 梦幻足球（Fantasy Premier League, FPL）是一个价值数十亿美元的产业，拥有数百万参与者。在固定预算的限制下，管理者需要选择最佳阵容以最大化未来的FPL积分。本研究旨在解决FPL阵容选择的优化问题，为参与者提供数据驱动的决策支持，以提高他们的游戏表现和潜在收益。

Method: 本研究将阵容选择问题公式化为数据驱动的优化问题，并开发了确定性和鲁棒混合整数线性规划模型。这些模型用于在满足预算、阵型和俱乐部球员数量（每个俱乐部最多三名球员）限制的条件下，选择首发十一人、替补阵容和队长。目标函数通过一个混合评分指标进行参数化，该指标结合了已实现的FPL积分和使用探索性数据分析技术识别出的比赛表现特征训练的线性回归模型的预测。研究还对包括简单平均、近期加权平均、指数平滑、ARIMA（自回归积分移动平均）和蒙特卡洛模拟在内的备选目标函数和成本估算器进行了基准测试。实验在2023/24赛季英格兰足球超级联赛的数据上进行。

Result: 在2023/24赛季英格兰足球超级联赛的实验中，结合约束预算和滚动窗口的ARIMA模型在样本外表现上最为稳定。加权平均和蒙特卡洛模拟方法也表现出很强的竞争力。研究发现，虽然鲁棒优化变体在某些目标上有所改进，但并非在所有情况下都优于确定性模型。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的框架通过数据驱动的优化方法，为梦幻足球（FPL）的阵容构建提供了透明的决策支持。实验结果表明，ARIMA模型结合特定约束条件在预测表现方面表现出色，为解决FPL中的关键决策问题提供了一种有效途径。该框架具有良好的扩展性，可以应用于FPL的芯片使用、多周转会规划以及动态队长选择等更复杂的场景，为FPL玩家和行业带来潜在价值。

Abstract: Fantasy football is a billion-dollar industry with millions of participants.
Under a fixed budget, managers select squads to maximize future Fantasy Premier
League (FPL) points. This study formulates lineup selection as data-driven
optimization and develops deterministic and robust mixed-integer linear
programs that choose the starting eleven, bench, and captain under budget,
formation, and club-quota constraints (maximum three players per club). The
objective is parameterized by a hybrid scoring metric that combines realized
FPL points with predictions from a linear regression model trained on
match-performance features identified using exploratory data analysis
techniques. The study benchmarks alternative objectives and cost estimators,
including simple and recency-weighted averages, exponential smoothing,
autoregressive integrated moving average (ARIMA), and Monte Carlo simulation.
Experiments on the 2023/24 Premier League season show that ARIMA with a
constrained budget and a rolling window yields the most consistent
out-of-sample performance; weighted averages and Monte Carlo are also
competitive. Robust variants improve some objectives but are not uniformly
superior. The framework provides transparent decision support for fantasy
roster construction and extends to FPL chips, multi-week rolling-horizon
transfer planning, and week-by-week dynamic captaincy.

</details>


### [95] [An Eulerian Data Assimilation Method for Two-Layer Quasi-Geostrophic Model in Physical Domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.14586)
*Hyeonggeun Yun,Quanling Deng*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为欧拉数据同化（EuDA）并结合条件高斯非线性系统（CGNS）的新方法，用于改进复杂物理系统的预测，尤其是在处理非线性动力学和多尺度变异性方面。该方法在模拟北极海冰漂流和涡旋恢复的简化物理域上进行了测试，通过数值求解两层准地转（QG）方程来评估。结果表明，EuDA-CGNS方法在细化时间步长和提高网格分辨率方面，性能指标（如RMSE和相关系数）得到持续改善，并且能够有效地捕捉耦合冰-海洋相互作用的多尺度流动特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的数据同化（DA）方法在处理具有非线性动力学和多尺度变异性的复杂物理系统时，尤其是在物理域中直接应用时，常常面临挑战。这主要是因为这些系统边界条件复杂且现象局部化、时变性强。因此，需要一种更有效的方法来整合观测数据和数值模型，以提高预测精度。

Method: 本研究开发了一种结合条件高斯非线性系统（CGNS）的欧拉数据同化（EuDA）方法。该方法在物理域内进行，能够处理非周期边界条件，并更直观地表示局部和时间相关的现象。研究以北极海冰漂流和涡旋恢复为例，使用两层准地转（QG）模型来模拟动力学。QG方程采用前向欧拉时间步进和中心有限差分格式进行数值求解。CGNS作为一种非线性滤波器，为非线性系统提供了一种解析和连续的滤波形式。模型性能通过事后均方根误差（RMSE）和模式相关性（Corr）进行评估。此外，研究还考察了一个耦合场景，其中海冰粒子在二维QG流和线性阻力作用下进行平流运动。

Result: 研究结果显示，EuDA-CGNS方法在细化时间步长方面，RMSE和Corr两个指标都得到单调改善。RMSE收敛到约0.1（即噪声强度），表明模型能够准确地估计系统状态。Corr值从0.64提升到0.92，表明随着网格分辨率的提高，模型对物理过程的模式捕捉能力显著增强。在耦合场景中，该框架成功捕捉了耦合的冰-海洋相互作用，证明了其在处理复杂系统动力学方面的灵活性和有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的EuDA-CGNS方法在物理域内有效地整合了数据同化和非线性滤波，解决了传统方法在处理非线性、多尺度和非周期边界条件系统时的局限性。通过在简化的北极海冰和涡旋模型上的成功应用，证明了该框架在提高预测精度和捕捉复杂流动特征方面的潜力。未来的工作可以进一步探索该方法在更复杂的真实世界系统中的应用，并考虑更精细化的模型和观测数据。

Abstract: Data assimilation (DA) integrates observational data with numerical models to
improve the prediction of complex physical systems. However, traditional DA
methods often struggle with nonlinear dynamics and multi-scale variability,
particularly when implemented directly in the physical domain. To address these
challenges, this work develops an Eulerian Data Assimilation (EuDA) method with
the Conditional Gaussian Nonlinear System (CGNS). The proposed approach enables
the treatment of systems with non-periodic boundaries and provides a more
intuitive representation of localized and time-dependent phenomena. The work
considers a simplified physical domain inspired by sea-ice floe trajectories
and ocean eddy recovery in the Arctic regions, where the dynamics are modeled
by a two-layer quasi-geostrophic (QG) system. The QG equations are numerically
solved using forward-Euler time stepping and centered finite-difference
schemes. CGNS provides a nonlinear filter as it offers an analytical and
continuous formulation for filtering a nonlinear system. Model performance is
assessed using normalized root mean square error (RMSE) and pattern correlation
(Corr) of the posterior mean. The results show that both metrics improve
monotonically with refining timesteps, while RMSE converges to approximately
0.1, which is the noise strength, and Corr increases from 0.64 to 0.92 as the
grid resolution becomes finer. Lastly, a coupled scenario with sea-ice
particles advected by the two-layer QG flow under a linear drag force is
examined, demonstrating the flexibility of the EuDA-CGNS framework in capturing
coupled ice-ocean interactions. These findings demonstrate the effectiveness of
exploiting the two-layer QG model in the physical domain to capture multiscale
flow features.

</details>
